</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I would trust Hagrid with my life.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s trust in Hagrid<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Professor Rubeus Hagrid</b> (b. <a href="/wiki/6_December" title="6 December">6 December</a> <a href="/wiki/1928" title="1928">1928</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> was an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, son of <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_father" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s father">Mr Hagrid</a> and the giantess <a href="/wiki/Fridwulfa" title="Fridwulfa">Fridwulfa</a>, and elder half-brother of the giant <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>.
</p><p>Hagrid attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> in <a href="/wiki/1940" title="1940">1940</a> and was sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house. In Hagrid's <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a>, he was framed by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> for the crime of opening the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and using his pet <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a> to attack several <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students and eventually killing <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">one of them</a>. Though <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_wand" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s wand">Hagrid's wand</a> was snapped and he was expelled, he was trained as <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">gamekeeper</a> of Hogwarts and allowed to live on the school grounds at the request of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, Hagrid was given the task of reintroducing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>. In 1993, Hagrid would assume the post of <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> professor after the retirement of <a href="/wiki/Silvanus_Kettleburn" title="Silvanus Kettleburn">Professor Silvanus Kettleburn</a>. As a member of both the original and the re-instated <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, Hagrid fought in several battles of the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding Wars</a>, including the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>. By <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, he was still living, and presumably still teaching and tending to his gamekeeping duties at Hogwarts, inviting Harry's son <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a> for tea when he joined the school as Harry informed him at the station, just as Hagrid had done to his father, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1928-1940)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281928-1940.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1928-1940)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1928-1940)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1928-1940)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>My dad was broken-hearted when she wen'. Tiny little bloke, my dad was. By the time I was six I could lift him up an' put him on top o' the dresser if he annoyed me. Used ter make him laugh...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid tells <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a> about his father<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/HP4-c24.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20150712193742" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HP4-c24.JPG" data-image-key="HP4-c24.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/HP4-c24.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150712193742" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/HP4-c24.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20150712193742" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/HP4-c24.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150712193742" decoding="async" width="200" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HP4-c24.JPG" data-image-key="HP4-c24.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/HP4-c24.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150712193742" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HP4-c24.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_father" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s father">his father</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was born on <a href="/wiki/6_December" title="6 December">6 December</a> <a href="/wiki/1928" title="1928">1928</a> to <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_father" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s father">Mr Hagrid</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fridwulfa" title="Fridwulfa">Fridwulfa</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giantess</a>, and grew up in the <a href="/wiki/West_Country" title="West Country">West Country</a> of <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, near the <a href="/wiki/Forest_of_Dean" title="Forest of Dean">Forest of Dean</a>, where he acquired his distinctive accent.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Hagrid was about three, his mother returned to her <a href="/wiki/Giant_colony" title="Giant colony">Giant colony</a>, leaving his father to raise him alone. Hagrid said he had very few memories of his mother from his childhood, but remembered his father fondly; as a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>, he overtook his father in size by the age of six, and amused the "tiny" wizard by picking him up and setting him on top of a dresser when Hagrid was annoyed with him. Later, when talking to Harry, Ron, and Hermione about the death of his mother, Hagrid admitted that she was not a great mother at all.<sup id="cite_ref-gof23_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gof23-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He grew to an height of eleven and a half feet tall, immense by human standards but very small by giant standards.
</p>
<h3><span id="School_years_at_Hogwarts_(1940-1942/43)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="School_years_at_Hogwarts_.281940-1942.2F43.29">School years at Hogwarts <span class="template-c">(1940-1942/43)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: School years at Hogwarts (1940-1942/43)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: School years at Hogwarts (1940-1942/43)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Tom Riddle</b>: "<i>Evening, Rubeus.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Rubeus Hagrid</b>: "<i>What yer doin’ down here, Tom?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Tom Riddle</b>: "<i>It’s all over. I’m going to have to turn you in, Rubeus. They’re talking about closing Hogwarts if the attacks don’t stop.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Rubeus Hagrid</b>: "<i>‘N at d’yeh —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Tom Riddle</b>: "<i>I don’t think you meant to kill anyone. But monsters don’t make good pets. I suppose you just let it out for exercise and —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Rubeus Hagrid</b>: "<i>It never killed no one!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Tom Riddle</b>: "<i>Come on, Rubeus. The dead girl’s parents will be here tomorrow. The least Hogwarts can do is make sure that the thing that killed their daughter is slaughtered…</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Rubeus Hagrid</b>: "<i>It wasn’t him! He wouldn’! He never!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Tom Riddle framing Hagrid for having opened the Chamber of Secrets<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221747" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom Riddle framing Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221747" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221747" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221747" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom Riddle framing Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221747" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Riddle finds Rubeus Hagrid keeping a young Aragog in the school dungeons, in <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid's father was thrilled when his son was accepted at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, where Hagrid began his education in <a href="/wiki/1940" title="1940">1940</a> in which he was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-house_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-house-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> During his <a href="/wiki/1940s" title="1940s">third year</a>, Hagrid acquired one in what would be a long line of dangerous <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_pets" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s pets">pets</a>: a young <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>, which he named <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>. 
</p><p>That same year, fifth-year student <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Marvolo Riddle</a>, who would go on to become Lord Voldemort, opened the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and unleashed another <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s basilisk">monster</a>, which Riddle used to attack and petrify a number of <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students until he finally caused the death of a girl named <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Myrtle Warren</a>. When the school was threatened with closing, a consequence highly undesired by Riddle, the boy found out about Aragog and turned Hagrid in as the culprit. It likely didn't help that Hagrid had a habit of getting into trouble every other week: he'd once tried raising <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> cubs under his bed and was known to sneak off into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> to wrestle trolls (both of these statements were likely exaggerations on Riddle's part however). Hagrid protected Aragog and helped him flee to the Forbidden Forest; however, he was shortly thereafter expelled from Hogwarts,<sup id="cite_ref-CoS_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CoS-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> a fate that he was relieved that his father never knew of, having died during Hagrid's second year.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following his expulsion, the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> forbade Hagrid from practising magic and destroyed his <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wand</a>. The then-<a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> teacher <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, who was convinced that Hagrid was innocent, nonetheless convinced then-Headmaster, <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, to have Hagrid trained for the job of <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Gamekeeper</a> and allow the orphan to remain a resident of the school. Hagrid continued to do magic using his <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_umbrella" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s umbrella">pink umbrella</a>, which most likely contained the broken fragments of his wand or perhaps even his entire wand intact. It may have been reconstructed for him by Dumbledore using the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>, although he only would have done this some years later, because he did not procure the Elder Wand until 1945.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="First_Wizarding_War_(1970-1981)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Wizarding_War_.281970-1981.29">First Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1970-1981)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970-1981)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970-1981)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>No, sir — house was almost destroyed but I got him out all right before the Muggles started swarmin' around. He fell asleep as we was flyin' over Bristol.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid to Dumbledore on rescuing young Harry Potter in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid as a member of the original Order</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime in the 1970s, Hagrid joined the original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. It was a secret organisation founded by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> to oppose <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. The Order was constructed after Voldemort returned to England from abroad and started his campaign to take over the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> and persecute Muggles and <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>. 
</p><p>Voldemort's first reign of terror lasted years and turned friends against each other. It was said that during this time it was difficult to trust one another, as you did not know for sure who had gone over to the dark side. The Order worked with the Ministry to oppose the Dark Lord and his followers, even allowing <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> the use of <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a>. Voldemort also had a number of magical dark creatures under his command as well, such as giants.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161208050449" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="140" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid delivers Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208050449" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161208050449" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208050449" decoding="async" width="250" height="140" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid delivers Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208050449" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid_delivers_Harry.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid delivering <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to 4 Privet Drive</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At the abrupt end of the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, Albus Dumbledore sent Hagrid to rescue a one-year-old Harry Potter from the ruins of his house in <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>, after Lord Voldemort <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">murdered</a> both <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a> in 1981. Using <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black%27s_motorcycle" class="mw-redirect" title="Sirius Black&#39;s motorcycle">Sirius Black's motorcycle</a>, he brought Harry Potter to Albus Dumbledore and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, who were waiting to deliver the boy to his only remaining family — Lily's <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> elder sister, <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia</a>, and her husband <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Vernon Dursley</a>. Hagrid was very sad at the thought of James and Lily Potter being dead.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Between_the_wars_(1981-1995)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Between_the_wars_.281981-1995.29">Between the wars <span class="template-c">(1981-1995)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981-1995)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981-1995)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery"><b>Unidentified seventh year</b>: "<i>Hagrid has saved my life on more than one occasion.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Unidentified first year</b>: "<i>Hagrid was the first person to welcome me to Hogwarts.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Unidentified students reminiscing on Hagrid's actions<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<h4><span id="Meeting_Jacob's_sibling"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_Jacob.27s_sibling">Meeting Jacob's sibling</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Meeting Jacob&#039;s sibling">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Meeting Jacob&#039;s sibling"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Early in the <a href="/wiki/1984%E2%80%931985_school_year" title="1984–1985 school year">1984–1985 school year</a>, Hagrid rescued <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">a student</a> from <a href="/wiki/Devil%27s_Snare" title="Devil&#39;s Snare">Devil's Snare</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He also met <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">Ben Copper</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Y1SQ_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Y1SQ-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Around this time, he also got <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">a puppy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly before one of his birthdays, Hagrid lost one of his pets, and stopped being as cheerful as he usually was.<sup id="cite_ref-Y1SQ_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Y1SQ-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Around this time, Dumbledore recruited Jacob's sibling to help throw him a huge birthday party to cheer him up and show just how much everyone appreciated him.
</p><p>At some point before this, he saved a seventh year's life, made a first year feel welcome at Hogwarts, and baked <a href="/wiki/Rock_Cake" class="mw-redirect" title="Rock Cake">Rock Cakes</a> to cheer up a third year.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_Harry_Potter">Meeting Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Meeting Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Meeting Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Hagrid</b>: "<i>If he wants ter go, a great Muggle like you won't stop him. Stop Lily an' James Potter's son goin' ter Hogwarts! Yer mad. His name's been down ever since he was born. He's off ter the finest school of witchcraft and wizardry in the world. Seven years there and he won't know himself. He'll be with youngsters of his own sort, fer a change, an' he'll be under the greatest headmaster Hogwarts ever had, Albus Dumbled—"</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Vernon Dursley</b>: "<i>I AM NOT PAYING FOR SOME CRACKPOT OLD FOOL TO TEACH HIM MAGIC TRICKS!"</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hagrid</b>: "<i>NEVER-INSULT-ALBUS-DUMBLEDORE-IN-FRONT-OF-ME!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hagrid threatening Vernon Dursley<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry_birthday.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141111131533" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry birthday.gif" data-image-key="Harry_birthday.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry_birthday.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141111131533" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry_birthday.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141111131533" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry_birthday.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141111131533" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry birthday.gif" data-image-key="Harry_birthday.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry_birthday.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141111131533" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_birthday.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid giving Harry a birthday cake</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Harry was accepted to Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, Hagrid was given the task of finding Harry, as Harry's uncle <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Vernon</a> was doing everything in his power to prevent his nephew from receiving his <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_acceptance_letter" title="Hogwarts acceptance letter">Hogwarts acceptance letter</a>. On Harry's <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_eleventh_birthday" title="Harry Potter&#39;s eleventh birthday">eleventh birthday</a>, Hagrid found the Dursleys and Harry in an extremely isolated <a href="/wiki/Hut-on-the-Rock" title="Hut-on-the-Rock">Hut-on-the-Rock</a>, and accidentally broke the door down from the force of his knocking, much to Vernon and <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia</a>'s intense displeasure; Vernon threatened him with a gun, demanding that he leave, only for Hagrid to contemptuously seize the gun and twist it into a knot like it was rubber.
</p><p>Not only did Hagrid show Harry some of the first real kindness he had ever known, bringing him a <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_birthday_cake_from_Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Harry Potter&#39;s birthday cake from Rubeus Hagrid">birthday cake</a> and generally caring about Harry's comfort and happiness in a way the Dursleys would never have even considered, but he also revealed to Harry that he was a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>. Hagrid several times came close to losing his temper with Vernon due to repeated insults against magic. He finally really lost it when Vernon dared to insult Albus Dumbledore, calling him a "crackpot old fool". In retaliation, he attempted to turn Harry's spoiled bully of a cousin, <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Human-to-pig_spell" class="mw-redirect" title="Human-to-pig spell">into a pig</a>, but only managed to give the boy a pig's tail. However, Hagrid credited this to Dudley being so much like a pig already, that there was not much left to do.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108044751" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Diagon Alley-Hagrid and Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108044751" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108044751" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108044751" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Diagon Alley-Hagrid and Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108044751" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Diagon_Alley-Hagrid_and_Harry.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Hagrid visit <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> in search of school supplies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once it was confirmed that Harry would be attending Hogwarts, after Hagrid decidedly ignored the Dursleys' protests, he helped Harry find his bearings in the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">magical world</a> by taking him to <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>, through the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a>, to buy his school necessities. While in Diagon Alley, Hagrid took Harry to <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a> to withdraw some funds from the Potters' <a href="/wiki/Vault_687" title="Vault 687">vault</a>, and to retrieve the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> from high-security <a href="/wiki/Vault_713" title="Vault 713">Vault 713</a>, to be transported to Hogwarts for even safer keeping. Hagrid also bought <a href="/wiki/Hedwig" title="Hedwig">Hedwig</a>, a snowy white owl, for Harry's eleventh birthday. He comforted Harry about his upcoming attendance at Hogwarts school and provided him with a <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express_ticket" title="Hogwarts Express ticket">ticket</a> detailing the date, time and place that he would need to catch the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>.
</p>
<h4><span id="Protecting_the_Philosopher's_Stone"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Protecting_the_Philosopher.27s_Stone">Protecting the Philosopher's Stone</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Protecting the Philosopher&#039;s Stone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Protecting the Philosopher&#039;s Stone"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Now, listen to me, all three of yeh — yer meddlin’ in things that don’ concern yeh. It’s dangerous. You forget that dog, an’ you forget what it’s guardin’, that’s between Professor Dumbledore an’ Nicolas Flamel —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid trying to convince the trio to stop nosing in about the Philosopher's Stone<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/HagridStranger.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070912093808" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="209" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HagridStranger.jpg" data-image-key="HagridStranger.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/HagridStranger.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20070912093808" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/HagridStranger.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070912093808" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/HagridStranger.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20070912093808" decoding="async" width="250" height="209" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HagridStranger.jpg" data-image-key="HagridStranger.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/HagridStranger.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20070912093808" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HagridStranger.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid and the stranger at the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When news got out that Vault 713 had been broken into (shortly after it had been emptied by Hagrid), Harry, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> quickly realised that whatever Hagrid had moved from <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> to Hogwarts was being hidden in the off-limits <a href="/wiki/Third-floor_corridor" title="Third-floor corridor">third-floor corridor</a> and guarded by a massive <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">three-headed dog</a>. Hagrid refused to disclose what the vault had contained, but he mentioned that the secret was "<i>between Professor <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> an' <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a></i>". In the spring of <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, Hagrid met a hooded man (<a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> in disguise) at the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a> and was enticed to play a game of cards when the mysterious person bet a <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragon</a> egg. Assuming the man was a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_dealer" title="Dragon dealer">dragon dealer</a> and fellow dangerous <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">creature</a> enthusiast, and under the influence of a fair amount of mead, Hagrid was convinced to divulge details about <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>, the three-headed dog Hagrid had lent to Dumbledore to help guard the Philosopher's Stone.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/A_Dragon_egg.png/revision/latest?cb=20180606144058" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="A Dragon egg.png" data-image-key="A_Dragon_egg.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/A_Dragon_egg.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606144058" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/A_Dragon_egg.png/revision/latest?cb=20180606144058" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/A_Dragon_egg.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606144058" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="A Dragon egg.png" data-image-key="A_Dragon_egg.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/A_Dragon_egg.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606144058" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:A_Dragon_egg.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The dragon egg preparing to hatch</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry, knowing that Hagrid had always wanted a dragon and thinking it far too much a coincidence that a man just happened to bring a rare dragon egg to the local pub, questioned Hagrid alongside Ron and Hermione about what had exactly happened during the card game. This time, Hagrid let slip to the trio what he had told the hooded man: the secret to calming Fluffy was that one simply had to play music and Fluffy would fall asleep. This allowed the trio to pursue the potential thief.
</p><p>Once the dragon egg hatched, Hagrid lovingly named the hatchling <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a>. Hagrid was initially blind to the chaos that the hatchling caused, but eventually, Harry, Ron, and Hermione convinced him to allow Norbert to be taken to a <a href="/wiki/Romanian_Dragon_Sanctuary" title="Romanian Dragon Sanctuary">dragon sanctuary</a> by friends of Ron's brother, <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>, who worked with dragons. After learning that Voldemort had attempted to steal the Stone using the information Hagrid gave him while drunk, Hagrid was distraught with guilt, but Harry assured Hagrid that he did not blame him. As an apology, Hagrid spent the time that Harry was unconscious sending off owls to some of his parents' old school friends, assembling an album full of wizarding photos of Harry's parents for him.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Imprisonment_in_Azkaban">Imprisonment in Azkaban</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Imprisonment in Azkaban">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Imprisonment in Azkaban"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>If anyone wanted ter find out some stuff, all they’d have ter do would be ter follow the spiders. That’d lead ‘em right. That’s all I’m sayin’.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid cryptically telling Harry and Ron how to uncover the truth<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Hagrid%27s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180219183350" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid&#39;s hut with visitors Malfoy Fudge Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid&#39;s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Hagrid%27s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180219183350" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Hagrid%27s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180219183350" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Hagrid%27s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180219183350" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid&#39;s hut with visitors Malfoy Fudge Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid&#39;s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Hagrid%27s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180219183350" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid%27s_hut_with_visitors_Malfoy_Fudge_Dumbledore.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Fudge visiting Hagrid in his hut in order to take him to Azkaban</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_school_year" title="1992–1993 school year">1992–1993 school year</a>, Hagrid showed public disdain for the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, although he never did so for any other teachers. In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> Hagrid was sent to the wizarding prison, <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, when the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> was re-opened. It was assumed he was the one who reopened the Chamber because his expulsion from Hogwarts was for the same occurrence. Even with <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> backing Hagrid, <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> insisted on taking Hagrid anyway. So on the same night Dumbledore was asked to step down as Headmaster by the school governors, Hagrid was escorted to Azkaban. However, he was able to help Harry and Ron solve the mystery surrounding the Chamber, by advising them to "<i>follow the spiders</i>."
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Follow the spiders. I’ll never forgive Hagrid. We’re lucky to be alive.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's anger at Hagrid's suggestion<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104163550" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="133" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Azkaban cutaway 300dpi-6.jpg" data-image-key="Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104163550" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104163550" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104163550" decoding="async" width="250" height="133" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Azkaban cutaway 300dpi-6.jpg" data-image-key="Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104163550" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Azkaban_cutaway_300dpi-6.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid during his short stint in Azkaban</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following the spiders led the boys to <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a> believed to have attacked students during the <a href="/wiki/1942" title="1942">1942</a>-<a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a> school year, and his <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Acromantula_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Acromantula colony">family</a>. Though Harry and Ron barely escaped the encounter with their lives, they managed to obtain some valuable information over the course of their conversation with Aragog: the monster within the Chamber had nothing to do with Hagrid, and the <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">girl</a> it had killed in the <a href="/wiki/1940s" title="1940s">1940s</a> had died in a bathroom. Harry was thus able to find the <a href="/wiki/Second-floor_girls%27_lavatory" class="mw-redirect" title="Second-floor girls&#39; lavatory">entrance</a> to the Chamber of Secrets, slay the <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">basilisk</a> within, and destroy <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s diary">Tom Riddle's diary</a>. As it turned out, the actual perpetrator had been the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">person</a> who had turned Hagrid in in 1943. Hagrid was exonerated and released from Azkaban. He returned to Hogwarts at three o'clock in the morning and joined in the ongoing celebration of the closure of what had been a terrifying incident, accidentally knocking Harry and Ron face-first into their plates of trifle when he cuffed them on the shoulders.<sup id="cite_ref-CoS_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CoS-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Protecting_Buckbeak">Protecting Buckbeak</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Protecting Buckbeak">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Protecting Buckbeak"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>S'all my fault. Got all tongue-tied. They was all sittin' there in black robes an' I kep' droppin' me notes and forgettin' all them dates yeh looked up fer me, Hermione. An' then Lucius Malfoy stood up an' said his bit, and the Committee jus' did exac'ly what he told 'em....</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid lamenting over his defence at Buckbeak's trial<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/B3C6M3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161220002522" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C6M3.jpg" data-image-key="B3C6M3.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/B3C6M3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161220002522" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/B3C6M3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161220002522" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/B3C6M3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161220002522" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C6M3.jpg" data-image-key="B3C6M3.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/B3C6M3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161220002522" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C6M3.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid's first Care of Magical Creatures lesson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/1993%E2%80%931994_school_year" title="1993–1994 school year">1993-1994 school year</a>, Hagrid became a professor of the <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>. For his first lesson, Hagrid taught his third-year students about <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriffs</a>. After explaining the proper way to greet a hippogriff and choosing Harry to demonstrate, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> caused trouble by insulting the hippogriff <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>, even though Hagrid had just warned the class to treat the creatures with respect. Buckbeak attacked Draco, and the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> issued an order for Buckbeak's execution after a hearing in which <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>'s pull at the Ministry was demonstrated, the incident also damaging Hagrid's self-confidence; later lessons focused on tamer creatures like flobberworms. Buckbeak's attack on Malfoy was later used during the Triwizard Tournament by Rita Skeeter to give Hagrid a very bad reputation. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bf/Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108220637" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak execution.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bf/Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108220637" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bf/Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108220637" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bf/Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108220637" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak execution.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bf/Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108220637" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter4-movie-buckbeak_execution.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The night of Buckbeak's intended execution</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>An appeal took place on 6 June 1994, but this was to no avail, and Buckbeak was to be executed at sunset that night. Before the execution, Harry, Ron, and Hermione visited Hagrid to console him, and they left just before <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">the executioner</a> arrived. Knowing Buckbeak's position, and the exact timing of the start of the execution, Harry and Hermione were able to save Buckbeak by going back in time with Hermione's <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a>, allowing them to rescue Buckbeak after the Ministry team sent to execute him had confirmed his location while Hagrid and Dumbledore were under observation, thus guaranteeing that neither would be blamed for Buckbeak's rescue/escape.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Delighted at the escape of his beloved pet, Hagrid spent the whole night celebrating with a large bottle of what may have been Firewhisky.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Triwizard_Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Triwizard Tournament">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Triwizard Tournament"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"'<i>Ow dare you! I 'ave nevair been more insulted in my life! '<a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">Alf-giant</a>? Moi? I 'ave —  I 'ave big bones!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Madame Maxime's words leaving Hagrid heartbroken<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210060913" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Care of Magical Creatures.jpg" data-image-key="Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210060913" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210060913" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210060913" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Care of Magical Creatures.jpg" data-image-key="Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210060913" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Care_of_Magical_Creatures.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid teaching his fourth year Care of Magical Creatures class</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/1994%E2%80%931995_school_year" title="1994–1995 school year">1994-1995 school year</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> was held at Hogwarts. Students from the <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a> attended Hogwarts starting in October, and Hagrid was tasked with taking care of the Beauxbatons' <a href="/wiki/Abraxan" title="Abraxan">Abraxans</a>, which drank only single malt whiskey and required forceful handling. Over the course of the year, he performed various tasks essential to the workings of the tournament: in November, he helped <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charles Weasley</a> take care of the <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragons</a> used in the First Task of the tournament, which he showed <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> at the suggestion of <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Professor Moody</a> (who was really <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>); he also bred <a href="/wiki/Blast-Ended_Skrewt" title="Blast-Ended Skrewt">Blast-Ended Skrewts</a> as a project for his fourth years, which were to be used in the Third task of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/Yull_ball_dancing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160516021242" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Yull ball dancing.jpg" data-image-key="Yull_ball_dancing.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/Yull_ball_dancing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160516021242" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/Yull_ball_dancing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160516021242" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/Yull_ball_dancing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160516021242" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Yull ball dancing.jpg" data-image-key="Yull_ball_dancing.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/Yull_ball_dancing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160516021242" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Yull_ball_dancing.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid at the Yule ball dancing with Madam Maxime</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Throughout the year, Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a>, the half-giantess headmistress of Beauxbatons, had a budding romantic relationship, which included dancing during the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>. Hagrid confided in her his life story, revealing to her that he is a half-giant, assuming her to be one as well because of her massive size. She was offended by the insinuations that she was part giant, and left him heartbroken.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rita Skeeter, in her <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> beetle form, overheard Hagrid's confession and <a href="/wiki/DUMBLEDORE%27S_GIANT_MISTAKE" title="DUMBLEDORE&#39;S GIANT MISTAKE">reported</a> it in the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i>. After receiving a fair amount of hate mail, Hagrid hid in the seclusion of <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_cabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s cabin">his hut</a>, while Professor <a href="/wiki/Wilhelmina_Grubbly-Plank" title="Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank">Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank</a> temporarily took over <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>, and attempted to resign from his position as Professor. Dumbledore refused to accept Hagrid's resignation, and he was eventually convinced to come back and teach by Harry, Ron, and Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Hagrid_with_trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108045039" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid with trio.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_with_trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Hagrid_with_trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108045039" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Hagrid_with_trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108045039" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Hagrid_with_trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108045039" decoding="async" width="250" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid with trio.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_with_trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Hagrid_with_trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108045039" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid_with_trio.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid in the Forbidden Forest with Ron and Hermione</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before the events of the third task, Hagrid was called by Dumbledore to escort Harry back to the castle after he and <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> encountered Barty Crouch Snr at the edge of the Forbidden Forest. When it appeared that Krum had been attacked by Crouch (really it was his son hiding in the trees), <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a> accused Dumbledore of treachery and spat at his foot. This caused Hagrid to lose his temper with Karkaroff and pin him to a tree, demanding an apology. He was talked down by Dumbledore, and saw Harry back to his common room, reprimanding him for being in such a situation and warning him against the foreign students.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the return of Lord Voldemort, Hagrid attempted to comfort Harry after his ordeal and admitted that he had believed Voldemort would have returned eventually, echoing something he had told Harry at their first meeting; that Voldemort did not have enough humanity left to die. He admitted to Harry and his friends that he and Madam Maxime had important business to attend to over the holidays but refused to say more. He also imparted some wisdom to Harry, helping him accept that what would come would come.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Second_Wizarding_War_(1995-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_Wizarding_War_.281995-1998.29">Second Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1995-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_to_the_Giant_colony"><a href="/wiki/Mission_to_the_Giant_colony" title="Mission to the Giant colony">Mission to the Giant colony</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Mission to the Giant colony">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Mission to the Giant colony"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Dumbledore wanted us ter take it very slow. Let’em see we kept our promises. We’ll come back tomorrow with another present, an’ then we do come back with another present — gives a good impression, see? An’ gives them time ter test out the firs’ present an’ find out it’s a good one, an’ get ’em eager fer more. In any case, giants like Karkus — overload ’em with information an’ they’ll kill yeh jus’ to simplify things. So we bowed outta the way an’ went off an’ found ourselves a nice little cave ter spend that night in, an’ the followin’ mornin’ we went back an’ this time we found Karkus sittin’ up waitin’ fer us lookin’ all eager.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid talks to Harry, Ron, and Hermione about his mission to try and appease the giants<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Giant_Colony.png/revision/latest?cb=20170210163301" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Giant Colony.png" data-image-key="Giant_Colony.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Giant_Colony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170210163301" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Giant_Colony.png/revision/latest?cb=20170210163301" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Giant_Colony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170210163301" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Giant Colony.png" data-image-key="Giant_Colony.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Giant_Colony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170210163301" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Giant_Colony.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid and Madam Maxime on their shared mission</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> learned of <a href="/wiki/Return_of_the_Dark_Lord" class="mw-redirect" title="Return of the Dark Lord">Voldemort's rebirth</a>, he sent Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Madame Maxime</a> as envoys to the <a href="/wiki/Giant_colony" title="Giant colony">giant colonies</a> of north-eastern <a href="/wiki/Minsk" title="Minsk">Minsk</a>, in the hopes of dissuading the giants from joining <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s side in the coming war. Bearing gifts of eternal <a href="/wiki/Gubraithian_Fire" title="Gubraithian Fire">Gubraithian Fire</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Goblin-made_battle_helmet" title="Goblin-made battle helmet">goblin-made battle helmet</a>, they eventually won over the <a href="/wiki/Gurg" title="Gurg">Gurg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Karkus" title="Karkus">Karkus</a>.
</p><p>However, two <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> that Voldemort had sent on the same mission engineered an uprising. This uprising was led by the giant <a href="/wiki/Golgomath" title="Golgomath">Golgomath</a>, who beheaded Karkus and usurped his position. Golgomath then ordered his subordinates to attack Hagrid and Maxime and forced them to flee. Golgomath was far more keen towards the Death Eaters and got on well with <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a>, both of whom enjoyed killing and had shared a dislike toward Hagrid. Hagrid subsequently found that his mother had died years ago, and the existence of his half-brother <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>, who was having a hard time within his colony as he was considerably smaller than most giants. Hagrid insisted on bringing Grawp back to Hogwarts due to this and presumably to prevent Grawp from being enslaved by Voldemort alongside the other giants. Grawp, however, was highly resistant to the idea and had a general tendency to be violent. Thus Hagrid and Grawp made the journey back to Scotland separately from Madam Maxime.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Living_with_Grawp">Living with Grawp</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Living with Grawp">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Living with Grawp"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Hermione, I couldn't leave him. See — he's my brother!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid explaining his decision to bring an undersized giant back to Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104160652" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid talking to the trio.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104160652" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104160652" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104160652" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid talking to the trio.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104160652" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid_talking_to_the_trio.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid telling Harry, Ron, and Hermione of his negotiations with the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giants</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>About halfway through the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">school year</a>, Hagrid returned from his mission for Dumbledore with his half-brother, <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> was brought in as the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, and later became the first and only <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">Hogwarts High Inquisitor</a>. Hagrid barely excused himself for his long absence from Umbridge's tyrannical questioning and was surprised that he would be subjected to her inspection soon afterwards.
</p><p>Hagrid resumed his teaching post, beginning with a lesson about <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a>. Despite their rather off-putting appearance and the inability of most of the class to see them, Hermione found these lessons far more useful than Hagrid's typical classes. Regardless, early in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Professor Umbridge put Hagrid on <a href="/wiki/Probation" title="Probation">probation</a> after supposedly finding his lessons unsatisfactory by her standards, despite Hermione's every effort to make sure Hagrid's curriculum was geared toward preparing students for the upcoming <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a>. Umbridge's harsh judgement was largely due to her distaste for "<a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a>," and it was only the resistance she met from Headmaster Dumbledore that kept her from firing Hagrid altogether. When confronted by the trio about this revelation, Hagrid attempted to make light of it (nearly concussing Professor Vector with his fist as she went past) but was consistently jumpy and nervous at the prospect of being sacked.
</p>
