<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180319043113" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid introduces the trio to Grawp.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180319043113" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180319043113" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180319043113" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid introduces the trio to Grawp.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180319043113" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid_introduces_the_trio_to_Grawp.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid introduces the trio to Grawp, his half-brother</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, once Dumbledore was forced to leave in order to shield Harry from punishment for establishing <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, Hagrid feared that he would be driven out by the new Headmistress Umbridge. In preparation for this, he introduced Harry and Hermione to Grawp. Grawp took an immediate liking to Hermione, whom he called "Hermy," and Hagrid asked the two of them, along with Ron, to take care of Grawp in his absence.
</p><p>Upon Dumbledore's departure, general chaos reigned within the school, as the students became determined to make Umbridge's job as hard for her as possible; <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jordan" title="Lee Jordan">Lee Jordan</a> even released a couple of <a href="/wiki/Niffler" title="Niffler">nifflers</a> into her office, for which she blamed Hagrid. Umbridge finally attempted to have Hagrid forcibly removed from the premises, and possibly arrested, when she brought several <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> officials to <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_cabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s cabin">his hut</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Ousting_of_Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Ousting of Rubeus Hagrid">middle of the night</a> so as not to cause a commotion with the students due to their earlier presence at <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>'s dismissal. Hagrid refused to go quietly and took on the officials, whose attempts to Stun him proved fruitless thanks to his giant blood. Fang came to his master's aid until one of the wizards Stunned him, prompting Hagrid to lift the culprit bodily from the ground and throw the unfortunate soul ten feet away.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706044702" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minerva wheelchair.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_wheelchair.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706044702" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706044702" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706044702" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minerva wheelchair.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_wheelchair.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706044702" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minerva_wheelchair.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid visiting a wheelchair bound McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While all of this was being witnessed by the trio's Astronomy exam, Professor <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> came charging out of the castle demanding that Hagrid be left alone and, in a disgustingly cowardly move, was seriously injured after being hit by four simultaneous <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spells</a> without warning. Enraged at this dishonourable conduct and the injury of his friend and colleague, Hagrid knocked out two more of his assailants before fleeing with his unconscious dog. <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> were sent to search for Hagrid, but he successfully evaded capture by hiding in the same <a href="/wiki/Cave_near_Hogsmeade" title="Cave near Hogsmeade">cave</a> that had previously proved a useful hiding place for <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>. Once Dumbledore was reinstated as the Headmaster of Hogwarts and Umbridge permanently removed from the school, Hagrid was welcomed back to his post.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Aragog's_funeral"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Aragog.27s_funeral"><a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Aragog" title="Funeral of Aragog">funeral</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Aragog&#039;s funeral">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Aragog&#039;s funeral"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>It's... Aragog... I think he's dyin'... he got ill over the summer an' he's not gettin' better...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid regarding a dying Aragog<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hagrid accompanied the trio and some members of the Weasley family to <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> as security for Harry, as these were dark and dangerous times. When Hagrid found out that none of his sixth-year Gryffindor students chose to continue past their <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> level of <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>, he initially misinterpreted this as a reflection of his students not liking him, as opposed to his questionable teaching.
</p><p>Hagrid eventually came to forgive Harry, Ron, and Hermione, understanding that their <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a> classes were difficult with massive work loads (and after Hermione confirmed that they could not have managed his classes with <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turners</a>, as they had all been smashed during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>); his anger abated completely when he was overcome with worry about the failing health of <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Halfblood-03189.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141227050826" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Halfblood-03189.jpg" data-image-key="Halfblood-03189.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Halfblood-03189.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141227050826" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Halfblood-03189.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141227050826" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Halfblood-03189.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141227050826" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Halfblood-03189.jpg" data-image-key="Halfblood-03189.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Halfblood-03189.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141227050826" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Halfblood-03189.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid at Aragog's funeral with Harry and Professor Slughorn</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Aragog died in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, he asked Harry, Ron and Hermione to help him bury the dead <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>'s body, though the heightened security around the castle with Voldemort's confirmed <a href="/wiki/Return_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Return of Lord Voldemort">return</a> made that difficult. Ultimately, spurred on by <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a>, Harry went to Hagrid's anyway and met Professor <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> on the way. Hagrid, along with Harry and Professor Slughorn, buried Aragog near the <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_pumpkin_patch" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s pumpkin patch">pumpkin patch</a>, and then gave him a tearful salute involving a good deal of mead. Harry used the situation to his advantage in retrieving a memory of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> asking about <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a> from a very inebriated Slughorn.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half Blood Prince">"<i>But what happened, Harry? I jus’ saw them Death Eaters runnin down from the castle, but what the ruddy hell was Snape doin’ with ‘em? Where’s he gone — was he chasin’ them?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid's confusion after the Battle of the Astronomy Tower<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half_Blood_Prince" class="mw-redirect" title="Harry Potter and the Half Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a></i></div></dd>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid carrying Dumbledore's body during his funeral</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> was killed by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> (on Dumbledore's orders). Near the end of the battle, he confronted <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a> who attempted to curse him only to realise that Hagrid's giant blood protected him. Rowle proceeded to set <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_cabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s cabin">Hagrid's hut</a> on fire while the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> were fleeing the school grounds. Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, who had chased Snape out of the castle, <a href="/wiki/Water-Making_Spell" title="Water-Making Spell">put it out</a> before the hut burned down. Hagrid was grief-stricken about Dumbledore's death, having been one of his strongest supporters. Hagrid carried Dumbledore's body to be interred at his funeral, almost breaking down several times, and later Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a> were seen comforting one another.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>My job's ter get you there safe, Harry!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid to Harry during the Battle of the Seven Potters, in response to Harry's protests that they turn around<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190818192131" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven potters.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190818192131" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190818192131" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190818192131" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven potters.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190818192131" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-seven_potters.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid and Harry Potter along with the others right before the sky battle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was among the thirteen members of the Order of the Phoenix, led by <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, that made up the <a href="/wiki/Advance_Guard" title="Advance Guard">Advance Guard</a>. The Advance Guard was in charge of <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">moving</a> <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> out of the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursley</a> home before his seventeenth birthday; the plan to do so included having five of Harry's friends (Ron, Hermione, <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</a>), as well as <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>, impersonate Harry to act as decoys, with an Order of the Phoenix member protecting each of them, and fly to six safe houses before taking portkeys to <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a>. Knowing that any Death Eaters watching out for them would assume the most skilled Auror would be moving with the real Harry, Alastor Moody took Mundungus Fletcher, while Hagrid was given the important task of protecting the real Harry in the side-car of <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black%27s_motorcycle" class="mw-redirect" title="Sirius Black&#39;s motorcycle">Sirius Black's motorcycle</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408223005" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Battle of the Seven Potters.gif" data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408223005" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408223005" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408223005" decoding="async" width="245" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Battle of the Seven Potters.gif" data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408223005" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort duelling against Harry Potter over Little Whinging</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> had helped Hagrid make several adjustments to the bike, including adding a button that produced dragon's fire, one that produced a net, and another that produced a solid wall, all of which materialised behind the bike by expanding out of its exhaust pipe. As it turned out, the Death Eaters had found out about the plan to move Harry earlier than rumoured (as the Order had purposely released false information about moving him at a later date) and the seven Harrys, with their Order protectors, were ambushed.
</p><p>Hagrid was able to keep the Death Eaters at bay with the help of the modifications on his bike and Harry's wand-work, but when Harry discovered one of the attacking Death Eaters was an <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">imperiused</a> <a href="/wiki/Stanley_Shunpike" title="Stanley Shunpike">Stanley Shunpike</a>, he made the unusual move of using the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a>. As he had done the same unexpected thing in <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_Little_Hangleton" title="Duel in Little Hangleton">Little Hangleton graveyard</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Harry was identified as the real deal, and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> came after him personally. In the struggle that followed, the motorcycle was torn apart and Hagrid dove off the bike at a Death Eater, falling a great distance to the ground. He survived, however, as did Harry, when it turned out they had fallen into the protection surrounding the <a href="/wiki/Tonks_house" title="Tonks house">Tonks house</a>.
</p><p>Nymphadora Tonks' parents, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Tonks" title="Edward Tonks">Ted</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">Andromeda Tonks</a>, healed their injuries, as Hagrid comforted Harry over the death of his beloved pet owl <a href="/wiki/Hedwig" title="Hedwig">Hedwig</a>, saying she had lived a "good old life." Since Hagrid had a history of having trouble keeping secrets, <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> suspected Hagrid was the one who had unintentionally leaked the date of the intended move, although Harry refused to blame anyone even before that was revealed not to be the case. That same night, Hagrid and all the other members of the Order mourned the death of Alastor Moody, who had been targeted immediately by Voldemort, exactly as Moody anticipated.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20101111083824" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid Olympe Maxime D H Wedding 1.jpeg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20101111083824" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20101111083824" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20101111083824" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid Olympe Maxime D H Wedding 1.jpeg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20101111083824" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rubeus_Hagrid_Olympe_Maxime_D_H_Wedding_1.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid attended Bill's and Fleur's wedding</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the summer of <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Hagrid was present at Harry's seventeenth birthday party. He gave him a <a href="/wiki/Mokeskin_pouch" title="Mokeskin pouch">mokeskin pouch</a> which held objects retrievable only by the owner. Hagrid also attended <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a>, accidentally sitting in the wrong spot (and destroying a number of chairs) before finding the correct place to sit.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> During the wedding, Kingsley Shacklebolt warned the crowd that Voldemort had taken over the Ministry. It is unknown if Hagrid fought the Death Eaters that attacked the Burrow.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hiding">Hiding</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hiding">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Hiding"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>We have heard within the last few hours, that Rubeus Hagrid, well known gamekeeper at Hogwarts School, has narrowly escaped arrest in the grounds of Hogwarts, where he has rumoured to have hosted a <a href="/wiki/Support_Harry_Potter_party" title="Support Harry Potter party">Support Harry Potter party</a>, in his house. However, Hagrid was not taken into custody, and is, we believe, on the run.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<i>Potterwatch</i> regarding Hagrid's escape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Once back at Hogwarts, Hagrid continued his job as gatekeeper and Professor of Care of Magical Creatures. At the request of new headmaster, Severus Snape, Hagrid was placed in charge of students who had been assigned detention. Detention with Hagrid consisted of work in the Forbidden Forest, which was far safer than detention with Amycus and Alecto Carrow. Later that year, Hagrid narrowly escaped arrest after holding a <a href="/wiki/Support_Harry_Potter_party" title="Support Harry Potter party">Support Harry Potter party</a> in his hut. He then went into hiding, presumably in the mountains, with his half-brother, Grawp. His escape was reported hours later on the radio programme <i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Heard You-Know-Who from up in our cave. Voice carried, didn’ it? “Yeh got ’til midnight ter gimme Potter.” Knew yeh mus’ be here, knew what mus’ be happenin’. Get down, Fang. So we come ter join in, me an’ Grawpy an’ Fang. Smashed our way through the boundary by the forest, Grawpy was carryin’ us, Fang an’ me. Told him ter let me down at the castle so he shoved me through the window, bless him. Not exac’ly what I meant, bu’ – where’s Ron an’ Hermione?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid to Harry, shortly before the start of the battle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104160953" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid carrying Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104160953" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104160953" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104160953" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid carrying Harry.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104160953" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid_carrying_Harry.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid carrying an apparently dead Harry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid returned to Hogwarts with <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a> for the final <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">battle</a>. He rushed out onto the grounds to prevent injury being done to the <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a> who had swarmed out of the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> and were climbing up the walls of the school. He was taken captive by the Death Eaters. When Harry appeared in the forest Hagrid shouted for him to run, though was silenced by Rowle. After Harry's apparent death at the Dark Lord's hands, Hagrid was forced to carry Harry back to the castle. As the supposed "victory party" approached the castle, Hagrid rebuked the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">centaurs</a> for refusing to involve themselves in the fight but was eventually reduced to sobs over the loss of Harry.
</p><p>When fighting resumed at the arrival of reinforcements, which included <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> and Hagrid's herd of tame <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a>, as well as the centaurs, Hagrid threw <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a> against the wall of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, possibly recognising him as <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>'s intended executioner. Hagrid was among the first to approach and congratulate Harry after Voldemort's ultimate defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> He was seen in the Great Hall among the other survivors of the battle.
</p>
<h3><span id="Later_life_(1998-)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Later_life_.281998-.29">Later life <span class="template-c">(1998-)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Later life (1998-)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Later life (1998-)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Don't forget Hagrid's invited you to tea next Friday.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry reminding Albus on his appointment with Hagrid<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Harry_hagrid_1998.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141111130811" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry hagrid 1998.gif" data-image-key="Harry_hagrid_1998.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Harry_hagrid_1998.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141111130811" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Harry_hagrid_1998.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141111130811" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Harry_hagrid_1998.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141111130811" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry hagrid 1998.gif" data-image-key="Harry_hagrid_1998.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Harry_hagrid_1998.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141111130811" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_hagrid_1998.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid hugs Harry after the battle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was still working at Hogwarts by <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, at 89 years old, owing to the natural longevity of wizardkind, which also meant that he would likely have an extremely long life by Muggle standards. He invited Harry and Ginny's youngest son, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a>, to his hut for tea, just as he had done during Harry's first year.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Hagrid never married, despite his reciprocated attraction to <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Madame Maxime</a>, as she was ultimately too sophisticated for them to be a good match.<sup id="cite_ref-Carnegie_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Carnegie-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/2019" title="2019">2019</a>, Hagrid led the members of the then recently established <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> seeking a career as <a href="/wiki/Magizoologist" title="Magizoologist">Magizoologists</a>, welcoming them by saying that he could sense they were going to sign in as he was able to see that they shared a curious spirit and ensuring them that, although being a Magizoologist was far from easy, they could succeed if they had the spirit to withstand the difficult trials and could recover. He first took them to the Diagon Alley to buy several robes and other essential pieces of equipment required to handle beasts and creatures for increased durability before proceeding to successfully teach the <a href="/wiki/Stamina_Charm" title="Stamina Charm">Stamina Charm</a>, (despite his own being "less-than-perfect"), and allowed them to help him handle several live <a href="/wiki/Fire_Crab" title="Fire Crab">Fire Crabs</a>. The primary takeaway they got from this, however, was a boost in their tolerance of pain.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> He also gave those who chose to became an Auror an elective to raise their defences against Beasts.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_description">Physical description</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical description">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Physical description"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>A giant of a man was standing in the doorway. His face was almost completely hidden by a long, shaggy mane of hair and a wild, tangled beard, but you could make out his eyes, glinting like black beetles under all the hair.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid's physical description<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Image40.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121111125119" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="344" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Image40.jpg" data-image-key="Image40.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Image40.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121111125119" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Image40.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121111125119" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Image40.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121111125119" decoding="async" width="250" height="344" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Image40.jpg" data-image-key="Image40.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Image40.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121111125119" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Image40.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rubeus Hagrid</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was born to a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> father and a <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giant</a> mother, making him a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>. As a half-giant, Hagrid possessed great physical strength and endurance, including a resilience against some <a href="/wiki/Spell" title="Spell">spells</a>, though his ability to withstand spells was not as great as that of full giants. He was about twice as tall as an average man, standing at eleven feet, six inches tall<sup id="cite_ref-LE_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LE-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> (too big for an ordinary-sized broomstick) and three times as wide, with a long mane of shaggy black hair and a beard that covered most of his face. Hagrid's hands were as big as dustbin lids and his feet in their boots were like baby dolphins.<sup id="cite_ref-hair_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hair-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> He had dark eyes that glinted like black beetles.<sup id="cite_ref-eyes_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eyes-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Hagrid's size often makes it difficult for him to enter rooms or buildings that are designed for ordinary sized people or not built with airy or grand designs, such as him not being able to fit easily into the Hospital Wing or the Burrow yet having no trouble moving in the Great Hall.
</p><p>He often wore an exceptionally large <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_moleskin_overcoat" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s moleskin overcoat">moleskin overcoat</a> with several pockets that held many things, though that sometimes caused him to spend a lot of time searching for what he wanted to find. Objects within the pockets have included any number of items, such as mouldy dog biscuits, the key to Harry Potter's <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> <a href="/wiki/Vault_687" title="Vault 687">vault</a>, peppermint humbugs, a squashy package of sausages, a copper kettle, a fire poker, wizard money, a birthday cake, birthday presents, a dirty spotted handkerchief, slug pellets, and a living owl. Hagrid's clothing is largely hand-made due to the descriptions of his clothing as being crafted of animal skin and far too large for a full-blooded or non-hybridised human being. 
</p><p>Despite his love for beasts, Hagrid was allergic to <a href="/wiki/Cat" title="Cat">cats</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I’m not saying his heart isn’t in the right place, but you can’t pretend he’s not careless.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> describing Hagrid's personality<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hagrid was an incredibly warm, kind-hearted man, and would often forget his exceptional size and strength when patting people on the back. Another of Hagrid's greatest traits was his courage. He was also very loyal to his friends and was ready to defend them or fight for them if necessary. He was particularly loyal to Albus Dumbledore, describing him as a "great man". He would react with fury if anyone dared insult the headmaster and wouldn't hesitate to magically assault or rough up the offender. However, despite his loyalty, Hagrid was not good at keeping secrets and accidentally told <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, the secret of how to get past his three headed dog, <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>, which all four of them used to get through to the Philosopher's Stone.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> This was again shown when he revealed his <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a> status to <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a>, which Harry, Ron and <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> all overheard, with the latter exposing it to the wizarding world by an article in the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6e/X_ddcb0bc4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180106104647" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="272" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="X ddcb0bc4.jpg" data-image-key="X_ddcb0bc4.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6e/X_ddcb0bc4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180106104647" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6e/X_ddcb0bc4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180106104647" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6e/X_ddcb0bc4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180106104647" decoding="async" width="180" height="272" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="X ddcb0bc4.jpg" data-image-key="X_ddcb0bc4.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6e/X_ddcb0bc4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180106104647" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:X_ddcb0bc4.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid in oven-mitts and an apron</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>C’mon, now, get a move on! Got a real treat for yeh today! Great lesson comin’ up! Everyone here? Right, follow me!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid's passion for magical creatures<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hagrid had a great love of magical creatures, including cross-breeds such as the <a href="/wiki/Blast-Ended_Skrewt" title="Blast-Ended Skrewt">Blast-Ended Skrewt</a>, and had a better relationship with most of the inhabitants of the Forbidden Forest than most people, including the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">centaurs</a>, though he had little interest in tame magical creatures due to the lack of a challenge they offered. Despite this, he did show a good understanding of such creatures when he returned to his post as <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> teacher, continuing lessons on <a href="/wiki/Unicorn" title="Unicorn">unicorns</a> after Professor <a href="/wiki/Wilhelmina_Grubbly-Plank" title="Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank">Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Unfortunately he tended to overlook the dangers behind certain magical creatures, such as his <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragon</a> <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-PS_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and his pet Acromantula <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, which was alleged by Tom Riddle to be the monster of <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Slytherin</a> in <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> resulting in Hagrid's expulsion from the school. Hagrid never spoke about why he was expelled and would ignore any inquiries about it. Hagrid was fond of creatures in general and seemed to want to own any creature was even slightly fierce — his desires included a <a href="/wiki/Warthog" title="Warthog">warthog</a> and any dragon that he could get his hands on. He tended to give his pets ironic names, such as Fluffy for a vicious three-headed dog, and Fang, an affectionate Boarhound.
</p><p>Hagrid had a fondness for drinks and was sometimes known to be aggressive, especially when people insulted or dishonourably attacked those he cared about. After <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Vernon Dursley</a> claimed that James and Lily Potter deserved their fates and called <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> a "<i>crackpot old fool</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-PS_19-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>, Hagrid threatened Vernon with his pink umbrella. When <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a> accused Dumbledore of treachery and spat at his feet, Hagrid lifted Karkaroff off the ground and slammed him against a tree, roaring at him to apologise to Dumbledore.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> When some <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> stunned <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, he was so disgusted that he attacked the Aurors in an uncontrollable rage, furiously denouncing them as cowards<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> and when he was younger, threw <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> to the ground when he framed Aragog of opening the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CoS_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CoS-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>  
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>It’s — all — my — ruddy — fault! I told the <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">evil git</a> how ter get past Fluffy! I told him! It was the only thing he didn’t know, an’ I told him! Yeh could’ve died! All fer a dragon egg! I’ll never drink again! I should be chucked out an’ made ter live as a Muggle!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid's deep emotional concern for Harry's safety<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Despite this, Hagrid was a very sensitive person and was known to burst into tears when someone close to him was harmed or killed, or when he felt responsible for something that put his friends in peril, such as drunkenly telling <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> how to get past his giant three headed dog, <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_19-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
His courage also concealed a deep fear of rejection and insecurity which was notably shown when he isolated himself after he was revealed as a half-giant and he attempted to resign from his position as the Care of Magical Creatures teacher until he was convinced otherwise by Dumbledore, Harry, Ron and Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>  
</p><p>When he was teaching, he also had a tendency to lose his self-confidence if his classes were disrupted such as when Buckbeak attacked Draco Malfoy, or if he believed people disliked his classes,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> which he mistook for people disliking him.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Although he overlooked certain dangers, Hagrid also avoided doing anything against the Wizarding Law when he was under pressure such as when he avoided setting Buckbeak free, fearing he would be put back in Azkaban,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and when he tried hard to avoid getting dangerous creatures when under probation by <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>  
</p><p>Hagrid was also a good and caring brother to <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>, insisting on bringing him back to Hogwarts on finding he was being picked on for his "small" stature by the other giants in his <a href="/wiki/Giant_colony" title="Giant colony">colony</a>, and hiding in the forest, despite the frequent injuries and the trouble doing so caused him.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He also enjoyed cooking for his friends. However, his tendency to mostly cook foods suitable for himself and a lack of understanding of what his friends preferred eating meant that his cooking was usually turned down politely.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_19-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Be grateful if yeh didn’t mention that ter anyone at Hogwarts. I’m — er — not supposed ter do magic, strictly speakin’.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid explaining to Harry his rare usage of magic<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif/revision/latest?cb=20150718195246" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid conjuring fire.gif" data-image-key="Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150718195246" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif/revision/latest?cb=20150718195246" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150718195246" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid conjuring fire.gif" data-image-key="Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150718195246" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid_conjuring_fire.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid conjuring fire with the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>For a man who was expelled during his third year and rarely used <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a> as a result, Rubeus Hagrid was a rather good <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, being considerably advanced, with some of his abilities even comparing to the N.E.W.T.-level academical difficulty. Being a Half-Giant, he also had magical abilities which stemmed from his giant blood, such as great superhuman strength and endurance along with a certain degree of magical resistance. Hagrid's hands-on and outdoor style of living allowed him to acquire other skills such as looking after magical creatures, craftsmanship, crossbowmanship and social networking within the magical community. 
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">Magical</a> aptitude</b>: Despite having never graduated from Hogwarts and therefore not being fully trained in the magical arts as well as probably not often practising magic as he wasn't allowed to do so technically in his own admission,<sup id="cite_ref-PS_19-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> as he had been expelled from Hogwarts and his wand was apparently destroyed some years earlier,<sup id="cite_ref-CoS_16-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CoS-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Hagrid's magical aptitude was clearly astonishing as he proved to be quite accomplished and skilled in magic enough that he was able to successfully conjure moderate levels of powerful magic. He was capable of performing successfully the majority of his spells using <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">non-verbal magic</a> via his umbrella and as his wand was apparently destroyed, he may also have been capable of <a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">wandless magic</a> as well, both of which only extremely powerful wizards and witches proved capable of using effectively. However, Hagrid's magic was never flawless as he was the only member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> who could not cast the extremely powerful and difficult <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a> and failed to completely transfigure <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a> into a pig, although he admitted that since Dudley was already so close to being a pig with his overweight physique and eating ways, he did not need to transfigure him completely, suggesting that Hagrid may have been able to do it but just chose not to further humiliate Dudley, and repair <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_motorbike" title="Harry Potter&#39;s motorbike">Sirius Black's motorbike</a> which had been heavily damaged during the Battle of the Seven Potters, though it must be noted that he was also struggling to control the motorbike and therefore he may just have been unable to exert enough magic to do so.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>He brought the umbrella swishing down through the air to point at Dudley — there was a flash of violet light, a sound like a firecracker, a sharp squeal, and the next second, Dudley was dancing on the spot with his hands clasped over his fat bottom, howling in pain. When he turned his back on them, Harry saw a curly pig’s tail poking through a hole in his trousers.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid attempting to turn Dudley Dursley into a pig<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Human_to_pig.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161011015440" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="96" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Human to pig.gif" data-image-key="Human_to_pig.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Human_to_pig.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161011015440" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Human_to_pig.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161011015440" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Human_to_pig.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161011015440" decoding="async" width="180" height="96" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Human to pig.gif" data-image-key="Human_to_pig.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Human_to_pig.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161011015440" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Human_to_pig.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid transfiguring Dudley Dursley</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Aguamenti_PM.png/revision/latest?cb=20161227030850" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="79" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Aguamenti PM.png" data-image-key="Aguamenti_PM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Aguamenti_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161227030850" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Aguamenti_PM.png/revision/latest?cb=20161227030850" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Aguamenti_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161227030850" decoding="async" width="180" height="79" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Aguamenti PM.png" data-image-key="Aguamenti_PM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Aguamenti_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161227030850" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Aguamenti_PM.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid conjuring water with Harry Potter</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Hagrid was at least moderately proficient in the field transfiguration, as shown in the Hut-on-the-Rock when he pulled off a partially successful transfiguration when he put a pig's tail <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a> in a failed attempt to <a href="/wiki/Human_to_pig_spell" title="Human to pig spell">transfigure</a> him into said animal. He could also perform <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjuration</a>; in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> he used the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a>, while in the Hut-on-the-Rock and in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> the <a href="/wiki/Water-Making_Spell" title="Water-Making Spell">Water-Making Spell</a>, to put out a fire in his hut during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>. This is fairly impressive, as Transfiguration is considered one of the most difficult branches of magic and even experienced wizards struggle with it. In the latter case, however, Harry had to inform him of the incantation for the spell, which Hagrid's response suggested he didn't correctly memorise.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Hagrid was also accomplished with <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a> as he could cast a <a href="/wiki/Rowboat_spell" title="Rowboat spell">spell</a> of his own that can enchant a boat to move on its own to a destination, which he used to transport himself and Harry back to the mainland from the Hut-on-the-Rock and used it on the Hogwarts boats to transport the first years across the <a href="/wiki/Great_Lake" title="Great Lake">Black Lake</a>. Hagrid was skilled in the <a href="/wiki/Engorgement_Charm" title="Engorgement Charm">Engorgement Charm</a> as he used it to enlarge his pumpkins to a giant size, his success impressing Hermione and Fred and George. Although he admitted to not having perfected it, he was competent enough in the <a href="/wiki/Stamina_Charm" title="Stamina Charm">Stamina Charm</a> to successfully instruct members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> who pursued a profession as a <a href="/wiki/Magizoologist" title="Magizoologist">Magizoologist</a> how to cast them.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_magic" class="mw-redirect" title="Nonverbal magic">Non-verbal magic</a></b>: Hagrid was quite skilled at using non-verbal magic, as shown when he both lit a fire non-verbally and transfigured a pig's tail on Dudley. These spells show that, even though Hagrid never graduated from Hogwarts, he had a powerful command of magic, as non-verbal magic was difficult to use (Hogwarts does not teach non-verbal magic until students are in their sixth year).</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i><a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a> will sometimes go for <a href="/wiki/Bird" title="Bird">birds</a>, of course, but Hagrid’s got the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Thestral_herd" title="Hogwarts Thestral herd">Hogwarts thestrals</a> well trained not to touch <a href="/wiki/Owl" title="Owl">owls</a> . . .</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Wilhelmina_Grubbly-Plank" title="Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank">Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank</a> complimenting Hagrid's gift for training magical beasts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a></b>: Hagrid was also extremely knowledgeable about magical creatures and was highly skilled in looking after, interacting with, and gaining their trust, including dangerous creatures which likely contributes from his experiences in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> and with his pets. Hagrid's skill and knowledge in handling creatures allowed him to be the <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> professor even though he was not a fully qualified wizard. Despite his skill and knowledge, many students considered Professor <a href="/wiki/Grubbly-Plank" class="mw-redirect" title="Grubbly-Plank">Grubbly-Plank</a> a more qualified teacher for the subject as Hagrid preferred teaching dangerous creatures and could lose his confidence if students tried to disrupt his classes or if he believed they did not like his classes. However, when Hagrid stopped dealing with dangerous creatures too much and began to become more experienced in teaching, his skills proved to be impressive enough to make him a reasonable teacher, as he proved to be able to improve all of the students excluding <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> view on him that they all expressed shock that <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> would sack him, although many of them did not choose to continue the subject for <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.Ts</a> due to their past experiences with the dangerous creatures he taught. The dangerous and unpredictable creatures which Hagrid taught included <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriffs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blast-Ended_Skrewt" title="Blast-Ended Skrewt">Blast-Ended Skrewts</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">thestrals</a>. Although he believed that tame and less harmful magical creatures did not pose many challenges, Hagrid neverthless possessed a remarkable amount of knowledge on them as well as monstrous creatures, enough that he was able to effectively continue Grubbly-Plank's lessons on <a href="/wiki/Unicorn" title="Unicorn">unicorns</a> and he also taught <a href="/wiki/Niffler" title="Niffler">nifflers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Flobberworm" title="Flobberworm">flobberworms</a>. Some of the creatures Hagrid looked after included a three headed dog named <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>, his pet <a href="/wiki/Boarhound" title="Boarhound">boarhound</a> <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a>, a baby <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragon</a> named <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a> named <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriff</a> named <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> and his half-brother <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>, who was a <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giant</a>. While his teaching methods were questionable, his knowledge helped Harry and his friends on numerous occasions, such as when they got past Fluffy while protecting the Philosopher's Stone, helped <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> escape on Buckbeak, faced a Blast-Ended Skrewt during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, and went to the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> using Thestrals. It should also be noted that his knowledge was such that he was initially the only person apart from Dumbledore who knew how to subdue Fluffy through music as even <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> was unable to get past Fluffy without getting injured, and <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, under Voldemort's influence, had to gather the secret from a drunken Hagrid on how to get past Fluffy (which Harry, Ron and Hermione later learnt) especially considering Voldemort and Snape were both already highly powerful and intelligent wizards even in their youths while Quirrell had experience with handling dangerous animals like trolls. Hagrid was skilled enough to gradually earn the respect and loyalty of Grawp, despite the protests of Harry, Ron, Hermione and Firenze, along with Grawp's violent nature. Hagrid's knowledge in dealing with giants and other dangerous magical creatures also made Dumbledore order Hagrid to go and attempt to recruit the giants to fight against Voldemort, which he would have succeeded if not for the Death Eaters' interference and <a href="/wiki/Golgomath" title="Golgomath">Golgomath</a>'s usurpation of the current Gurg, <a href="/wiki/Karkus" title="Karkus">Karkus</a>. Due to his friendship with Aragog, Hagrid was the only person who was able to visit the Acromantula tribe in the Forbidden Forest without being harmed, although this was lost after Aragog's death. Up until he rescued <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">Forbidden Forest Centaur colony</a>, Hagrid was among the very few that they respected and trusted, as he was able to visit them and interact with them cordially and <a href="/wiki/Torvus" title="Torvus">Torvus</a> even noted that Hagrid held enough influence that if <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> was a friend of Hagrid, the Centaurs would consider trusting them as well and it was his advice that eventually allowed the student to earn their respect. Grubbly-Plank also noted that Hagrid had the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Thestral_herd" title="Hogwarts Thestral herd">Hogwarts thestrals</a> well trained so that they didn't touch owls even though they were noted to have occasionally gone after birds. This talent also helped him as he was trusted with leading the <a href="/wiki/Magizoologist" title="Magizoologist">Magizoologist</a> faction of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> and had efficiently taught the recruits how to handle beasts safely. This can all indicate that Hagrid was a considerably talented person on the subject and this was clearly his strongest subject, possessing more knowledge than even wizards who were more powerful and intelligent, despite lacking the qualifications along with the teaching experience and understanding to fully engage his students.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Altough not a well known skill of his and his actual level as a potion maker is unknown, Hagrid displayed a remarkable amount of knowledge in the subject. When he asked <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> to brew the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Breathing_Potion" title="Fire-Breathing Potion">Fire-Breathing Potion</a> in order to burn the Devil Snare holding Fang in the year 1985, he was able to thoroughly explain to the student all the ingredients needed to brew the potion and was aware that mint had cooling properties that would allow them to consume it without harming themselves.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Superhuman_strength" title="Superhuman strength">Superhuman strength</a></b>: Due to his giant blood, Hagrid possessed great levels of superhuman strength, as shown when <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Vernon Dursley</a> threatened Hagrid with a gun and Hagrid responded by easily twisting his gun to a knot as if the gun was made of rubber. Hagrid's great strength was also shown when, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, he threw Walden Macnair across the Great Hall, a space which can easily fit all the students and staff at Hogwarts. The great strength of Hagrid was also seen whenever he tried to gently pat someone on the back, an act which usually sent the recipient flying. His strength also helped, given the kind of creatures he tended to look after, such as Fluffy, a gigantic three-headed dog, a 10-foot long Blast-Ended Skrewt and <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a> the size of a small elephant (though seeing as he was Hagrid's friend, he might not have been that bad to look after). Hagrid's strength also proved to be a big advantage when in battle and a powerful blow from Hagrid could badly injure and knock a person unconscious instantly as shown during his battle with some <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>. It is also possible that Hagrid was capable of killing a person or animal with powerful blows from his great strength alone, although this was rarely shown as conflicts with enemies were rare for Hagrid. Given Hagrid's absurd ease in handling creatures as large as Acromantulas, three-headed dogs, and his half-brother, Grawp, it can be safe to assume that Hagrid is capable of lifting well over ten-thousand pounds and exerting far more force in combat. Hagrid was also able to control Madame Maxime's horses which were each described as being the size of an elephant and required forceful handling. Hagrid's own massive size would take extreme power just to be able to move, so for him to be able to move as effortlessly as he does, let alone exert his strength as he does must mean that his strength is enhanced by magical means as well as physical. In fact, his strength was such that he was described to have wrestled <a href="/wiki/Troll" title="Troll">trolls</a> in the Forbidden Forest <i>as a boy</i>. Hagrid also regularly hauls in the massive Hogwarts Christmas trees simultaneously by himself with no discernible strain, even though each one weighs at least several thousand pounds based on their described height and probable species. Based on this, the full extent of Hagrid's superhuman strength, while never seen explicitly in the series, most certainly makes him a force of nature in his own right.</li>
<li><b>Superhuman endurance</b>: Hagrid is also known for being able take quite a beating. Due to his outdoorsy line of work, Hagrid is able to exert himself at the peak of his superhuman strength for hours at a time without any known limits to how long he can maintain his stamina.
