Given that he is capable of keeping up with tutoring and taming his full-giant half-brother, Grawp, and still keep up with his lessons as a Hogwarts Professor, his duties as gamekeeper, maintaining a social life, and his various hobbies of tending to and caring for injured and sick animals in the Forbidden Forest, all while nursing injuries from Grawp, Hagrid certainly has vast levels of superhuman stamina that no other character has matched in the series. Hagrid's bodily tissues are also extremely strong, enhanced due to his giant blood, allowing him to endure beatings from his half-brother that would absolutely kill any ordinary man, regardless of their physical conditioning, although he still experienced visible and rather nasty wounds in the form of bruising and various minor cuts and lacerations throughout his body. Hagrid is also capable of withstanding torture from the likes of Voldemort and his Death Eaters, as evidenced by his maintaining of full consciousness after being captured during the first half of The Battle of Hogwarts.</li>
<li><b>Magical resistance</b>: Hagrid was resistant to stunning spells because of his giant blood. This also gave Hagrid some protection against curses, including moderate levels of <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Magic</a> as even the Death Eaters attempts to curse him after Dumbledore's death failed, which gave him an advantage whenever he was involved in a battle.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">Poison</a> resistance</b>: Due to Hagrid's work with various magical creatures, many of which are venomous and highly likely to carry disease, it can be assumed that Hagrid's magical resistance afforded him a degree of foreign chemical resistance as well. This can also be assumed in part due to his enormous size in accordance with his giant heritage, as toxicity in the body is relative to one's size and the amount of a foreign substance circulating within. This can also be seen in his difficulty with becoming intoxicated, as it took Quirrell several hours to get Hagrid drunk enough to divulge the information of how to get past Fluffy in the first chamber in 1992. In fact, Hagrid's resistance to alcohol toxicity was so strong that he was able to down an entire bottle of brandy in a single swig without any notable effects on his behaviour or cognitive functioning following the Battle of the Seven Potters in 1997. Such a feat would likely be impossible for anyone of entirely human heritage without the aid of magic.</li>
<li><b>Arbalist skills</b>: Hagrid was also a skilled crossbowman, a crossbow being his primary means of defence.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">Physical combat skills</a></b>: Hagrid was highly proficient at fighting physically. This was displayed in 1996 when Hagrid was attacked by <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, along with some Aurors, who attempted to sack and arrest him. Hagrid managed to physically defeat all the Aurors effortlessly, which enabled him to escape from Umbridge. It should be noted that his combat was such that even Umbridge's remaining Auror was hesitant to attack Hagrid. Before that, he also rescued <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a> from the other centaurs in the Forbidden Forest after they attempted to kill him for accepting a <a href="/wiki/Divination_(class)" title="Divination (class)">teaching post</a> in Hogwarts and escaped from the entire Acromantula colony of the Forest to give Aragog a proper burial all without any injuries, which is another testament to Hagrid's combat skills especially as both centaurs and acromantulas were powerful creatures in their own right. Also, in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Hagrid easily physically defeated <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a> by throwing him across the Great Hall and he survived the battle. As Hagrid rarely used magic, he normally relied on these skills, his great strength, magical and physical endurance and possibly his crossbowman skills to fight in a battle and presumably used his skills to participate in the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First</a> and <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding Wars</a> when he was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. However, he did occasionally use his umbrella-concealed wand when battling, indicating that he was willing to use magic against his opponents alongside his physical battling abilities when the time was right.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Gamekeeping skills</a></b>: Hagrid began his training as a Hogwarts Gamekeeper in 1943 after his third-year expulsion, possibly under Gamekeeper <a href="/wiki/Ogg" title="Ogg">Ogg</a>; it is known he would have been Ogg's assistant during the 1960s. Hagrid most likely was an efficient and skilled Keeper of Keys and Grounds as there was no mentioned blunder, replacement or substitute (with the exception of Professor <a href="/wiki/Grubbly-Plank" class="mw-redirect" title="Grubbly-Plank">Grubbly-Plank</a> on two occasions) throughout his time in this position, and was able to keep up this position alongside his teaching duties as the Care of Magical Creatures professor and his duties for the Order of the Phoenix. These duties included escorting first-year students to Hogwarts, looking after the school keys, preparing for the <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en_Feast" title="Hallowe&#39;en Feast">Hallowe'en</a> and <a href="/wiki/Christmas_Feast" title="Christmas Feast">Christmas</a> feasts by preparing the pumpkins and Christmas trees respectively, performing secret and special tasks for the other Hogwarts teachers, and tending to matters which would be difficult for ordinary people and wizards to do such as tending to matters in the Forbidden Forest and looking after the magical creatures around the Hogwarts grounds.</li>
<li><b>Cooking skills</b>: Living alone in his cabin, Hagrid cooked for himself, though he would have meals in the Great Hall on occasion, such as the various school feasts. He apparently enjoyed his own food, though, being a half-giant, his tastes often clashed with those of his guests. He has been known to serve such foodstuffs to his guests as <a href="/wiki/Rock_cake" title="Rock cake">rock cakes</a> that were too hard for a normal human to chew and a "<a href="/wiki/Casserole" title="Casserole">beef casserole</a>" that was actually made of some taloned creature. Guests used to his cooking would often respectfully decline his food, even if it was something of his they had never tried, such as when Harry and Ron turned down some <a href="/wiki/Bath_bun" title="Bath bun">Bath buns</a> he had made in 1994. However, one occasion when his cooking was appreciated was when he cooked some sausages for Harry the first time they met at the Hut-On-The-Rock, which Harry noted was tastier than anything he had eaten before starting Hogwarts.</li>
<li><b>Tactical thinking and resourcefulness</b>: Hagrid was also good both at being resourceful and thinking tactically when he was in a serious situation. When <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a> was accused of being <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">Slytherin's Monster</a>, Hagrid sent him to the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> to protect him, knowing it was the only safe place for him when Hagrid was expelled on suspicion of opening the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, also preventing Hagrid from getting in further trouble for his possesion of the Acromantula. This was again shown before he was temporarily sent to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> when he sent a coded message to Harry and Ron, indirectly telling them to visit Aragog which, while it was almost fatal, allowed them to discover that Hagrid was innocent and determine the location of the Chamber of Secrets, in turn also resulting in Hagrid's release from Azkaban. Another instance is when he smuggled Grawp into the Forbidden Forest without even Umbridge's attention and tactfully brought Harry and Hermione to see him while the Quidditch Final was taking place, ensuring a distraction for the other Hogwarts residents. He also successfully escaped capture on two occasions by fleeing to the same cave Sirius Black and Buckbeak temporarily lived in: first was when Umbridge tried to get him both sacked and arrested due to her prejudice against Hagrid, and the second was when he was almost caught by the Death Eaters for holding a <a href="/wiki/Support_Harry_Potter_party" title="Support Harry Potter party">Support Harry Potter party</a> during Voldemort's control over Hogwarts, taking Fang with him for both occasions and Grawp on the second occasion. He was also able to successfully determine that Voldemort was going to wage war on Hogwarts when he heard his message to surrender Harry from his cave, allowing him, Grawp and Fang to return to Hogwarts in time before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> began. His resourcefulness was also demonstrated when he used a <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_moleskin_overcoat" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s moleskin overcoat">moleskin overcoat</a> to carry most of his possessions while travelling, which would be useful in more serious situations if he had to fight in a battle during which he would be unable to carry the majority of his possessions by hand.</li>
<li><b>Extreme dexterity</b>: Given Hagrid's superhuman size and strength, his dexterity and coordination is well above average considering he is able to handle people and objects that are extremely delicate and fragile, such as Harry when he was just a baby without the slightest bit of difficulty. This level of control over his massive form is to the extent that he is able to weave bindings from stray unicorn tail hairs to secure bandages and splints on injured animals that he finds in the Forbidden Forest. Given that unicorn tail hair is an unusually fine material, Hagrid must have amazingly deft hands to be able to craft it in such a way. His lack of control over his strength is usually in response to his emotions, but it can be assumed that given a moment to concentrate he can control his massive bulk enough to achieve incredible manual feats.</li>
<li><b>Craftsmanship skills</b>: Due to Hagrid's hands-on style of living, he has developed great skill at building or creating things by hand, such as his clothes, his cabin, and various other items. He is a fine whittler as he crafted a flute from wood that he gave Harry for his first Christmas at Hogwarts that when played made a sound like an owl. He likely also made his commonly worn moleskin overcoat that contains a wide variety of items. Hagrid also likely built the pen that he used to hold the hippogriffs for his first lesson as Professor of Care of Magical Creatures, in autumn of 1993.</li>
<li><b>Social networking</b>: Due to Hagrid's work in the Order of The Phoenix and his skills at negotiating and making great connections within the magical community, especially with creatures of great pride such as the centaurs, he has great ability to make allies. Dumbledore specially chose Hagrid for this skill to be an envoy to the giants during the summer of 1995. Despite his lack of success due to the Death Eaters' interference and Golgomath's usurpation of the current Gurg, Karkus, Hagrid had great initial strides with the giant colony, showing his impressive social aptitude with magical creatures and beings of all levels of sapience and intellect. He also indirectly convinced the centaurs to fight alongside the reinforcements during the second half of the Battle of Hogwarts after verbally admonishing them for their apparent cowardice, eventually resulting in the defeats of many Death Eaters.</li>
<li><b>Musical skills</b>: While not a very well known skill of his, Hagrid has shown adequate aptitude for music and would sing while enjoying a drink at events like Bill and Fleur Weasley's wedding and after Aragog's funeral. He also possessed enough skill in the area to create the wooden flute he gave Harry for Christmas in 1991, which when played created music that sounded a lot like the hooting of owls. His aptitude in music also helped him when dealing with certain magical creatures, such as being capable of playing a good enough music to easily make Fluffy fall asleep in order to calm him.</li>
<li><b>Teaching skills</b>: At first, due to his nervousness, teaching inexperience and desire to teach more dangerous magical creatures due to believing their greater quality, Hagrid was a poor teacher and his teaching ability was disliked by all, with only Harry, Hermione and Ron supporting him. In his first year as a teacher, his teaching ability was also hampered due to his first lesson being disrupted by Draco Malfoy, along with his concern over Buckbeak's safety after he attacked Malfoy for insulting him. However, over time as he gained more experience and started to teach more excitable creatures, he became good enough that although many of them still chose not to continue Care of Magical Creatures in their N.E.W.Ts, all but Slytherin students no longer complained as much about his teaching and openly admitted Hagrid's improvement, defending his teaching skills when he was sacked by <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, which was to be expected from Umbridge's prejudice towards magical creatures, and expressing shock that it happened. By <a href="/wiki/2019" title="2019">2019</a>, Hagrid had clearly improved reasonably, as he was trusted with teaching members of the highly important <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> who wanted to become Magizoologists and was able to do so succesfully, ranging from teaching the <a href="/wiki/Stamina_Charm" title="Stamina Charm">Stamina Charm</a>, despite his less-than-perfect version, and giving them an effective elective regarding magical creatures.</li>
<li><b>Leadership skills</b>: Although mostly taking orders from Dumbledore and after he was gone the other professors, by 2019, Hagrid had clearly became at least a competent enough leader to be trusted with handling the Magizoologist faction of the Statute of Secrecy Task Force, which clearly shows considerable leadership, being able to lead a rather large amount of magical beast handlers into handling Foundables that included Beasts without attracting the attention of Muggles.</li></ul>
<h2><span id="Hagrid's_pets"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hagrid.27s_pets">Hagrid's pets</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hagrid&#039;s pets">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Hagrid&#039;s pets"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_pets" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s pets">Rubeus Hagrid's pets</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 132px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/Hagrid_l.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180106104508" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="130" height="201" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid l.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_l.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/Hagrid_l.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/130?cb=20180106104508" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/Hagrid_l.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180106104508" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/Hagrid_l.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/130?cb=20180106104508" decoding="async" width="130" height="201" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid l.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid_l.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/Hagrid_l.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/130?cb=20180106104508" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid_l.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid with <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As early as in his <a href="/wiki/1940s" title="1940s">third year</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, and possibly earlier than that, Hagrid managed to gain possession of numerous magical creatures, many of them dangerous, including <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a> (later Norberta). Hagrid's love for animals and his talent for taming and training them won him the post of <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> Professor at Hogwarts.
In their fourth year, Harry and his classmates were expected to help take care of Hagrid's <a href="/wiki/Blast-Ended_Skrewt" title="Blast-Ended Skrewt">Blast-Ended Skrewts</a>, one of which (grown to an enormous size) was placed in the hedge maze for the final task of the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>She wasn' really the maternal sort. Well ... it's not in their natures, is it?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid discussing his <a href="/wiki/Fridwulfa" title="Fridwulfa">mother</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/34272-26957.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090304184852" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="34272-26957.gif" data-image-key="34272-26957.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/34272-26957.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090304184852" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/34272-26957.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090304184852" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/34272-26957.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090304184852" decoding="async" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="34272-26957.gif" data-image-key="34272-26957.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/34272-26957.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090304184852" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:34272-26957.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>, his half-brother</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rubeus Hagrid was born to <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_father" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s father">Mr Hagrid</a>, a wizard, and the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giantess</a> <a href="/wiki/Fridwulfa" title="Fridwulfa">Fridwulfa</a>. Fridwulfa left the family because her son was "too small" for her liking, though Hagrid never seemed to resent her for abandoning him, generally appearing relatively indifferent about his lack of relationship with her. His father, on the other hand, seemed to be a very caring man who was heartbroken when his wife left, and was amused by the fact that, at the age of six, Hagrid was large enough to be able to set him on top of a dresser.<sup id="cite_ref-gof23_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gof23-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Mr Hagrid died when his son was twelve years old, and by the time Hagrid tried to find his mother in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, she too had died, although he dismissed the issue on the grounds that he barely remembered her. On the other hand, he was saddened by his father's death, though he was at least glad that his father did not live to see Rubeus expelled from school.
</p><p>During his travels to the Northern <a href="/wiki/Giant_colony" title="Giant colony">giant colonies</a> that same year, Hagrid found his maternal half-brother: an undersized giant called <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>. As Grawp's size made it difficult for him to function within his colony, Hagrid brought him back to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and hid him within the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>. As Hagrid and Maxime's mission had failed, it is extremely likely that Hagrid also brought Grawp back to prevent his half-brother from being enslaved by Voldemort alongside the other giants. Hagrid's attempts to raise and socialise Grawp initially appeared completely pointless; Grawp's progress in picking up English, or in curbing his violence, which often left Hagrid with a number of painful looking injuries, seemed almost non-existent.
</p><p>However, over the course of the year, Grawp grew increasingly attached to his older brother and was distressed by Hagrid's disappearance after <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> attempted to have Hagrid arrested in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> By <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">funeral</a>, Grawp was relatively calm and presentable, and he even attempted to comfort Hagrid by patting him (though a bit too hard) on the head and later embracing him.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_25-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Grawp spent the first part of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> stumbling around, yelling for "Hagger," but eventually jumped into the fray, fighting the giants brought to the battle by Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_26-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pets_and_other_creatures">Pets and other creatures</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Pets and other creatures">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Pets and other creatures"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Buckbeak_Pottermore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161205032522" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Buckbeak Pottermore.png" data-image-key="Buckbeak_Pottermore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Buckbeak_Pottermore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161205032522" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Buckbeak_Pottermore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161205032522" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Buckbeak_Pottermore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161205032522" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Buckbeak Pottermore.png" data-image-key="Buckbeak_Pottermore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Buckbeak_Pottermore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161205032522" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Buckbeak_Pottermore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> the <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriff</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid had a good relationship with most of his pets and other magical creatures, most notably <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>. His relationship with most magical creatures was arguably better then the ones most other wizards had. 
</p><p>Fang was usually Hagrid's companion most of the time, although he was cowardly. Fang demonstrated some protectiveness towards Hagrid in spite of his cowardly nature such as when he attempted to protect Hagrid when Dolores Umbridge and some Auror's attempted to sack and arrest him. Hagrid, in turn, was also protective of Fang as he was enraged when the Aurors had stunned him, carrying his unconscious body as he fled Hogwarts, and immediately went after Fang when he was afraid during the Battle of Hogwarts. 
</p><p>Hagrid had a huge friendship with Aragog, whom he had hatched in an egg when he was a student at Hogwarts. Hagrid protected Aragog when he was suspected to be the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">monster</a> that opened the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, throwing <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> to the ground when he tried to curse him and sending Aragog to live in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>. Hagrid managed to find Aragog a wife, <a href="/wiki/Mosag" title="Mosag">Mosag</a>, which allowed Aragog to have a family in the forest. Aragog, in turn, was grateful for Hagrid's friendship and protection to the point that he never directly harmed a human out of respect for Hagrid and commanded his family not to harm Hagrid while he was alive. However, this did not stop Aragog from letting his children and descendants attempt to eat Harry and Ron even though they were friends of Hagrid, claiming that he could not deny them fresh meat when it wandered into their midst. Hagrid was devastated when Aragog died and, along with Professor Slughorn, buried him near his Hut. Although Aragog's children and descendants did not hold back in attempting to devour Hagrid after Aragog's death, Hagrid attempted to protect them during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> in honour of his friendship with Aragog, even though the Acromantulas were attacking both Death Eaters and Hogwarts defenders.
</p><p>Hagrid cared greatly about Buckbeak as he tried hard to prevent his execution by the Ministry of Magic and was overjoyed when he managed to escape with <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>. Hagrid also looked after Buckbeak after Sirius was killed by Bellatrix. Hagrid briefly had a pet dragon named <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a>, although since dragons were illegal, Hagrid reluctantly allowed Norbert to be sent to Charlie in Romania. Hagrid also owned a three-headed dog named <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>, although it is unknown what relationship he had with him.
</p><p>Hagrid also had a cordial relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">Forbidden Forest Centaur colony</a>, especially with <a href="/wiki/Bane" title="Bane">Bane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronan" title="Ronan">Ronan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magorian" title="Magorian">Magorian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a>, and sometimes visited them whenever he went inside the Forest. However, Hagrid had a falling out with the centaurs when he defended Firenze from them as they believed Firenze had betrayed them by accepting the teaching post of <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> at Hogwarts, which was further complicated when he brought Grawp into the Forbidden Forest. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, when Hagrid carried Harry, believing he was dead, back to Hogwarts, he was furious when the centaurs did not fight in the first half for Harry, accusing them of cowardice, which convinced them to fight in the second half of the battle. While Hagrid remained on good terms with Firenze, it is unknown whether Hagrid made peace with the other Centaurs after the battle ended.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Great man, Dumbledore. 'S long as we've got him, I'm not too worried.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid discussing his trust in Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, his dear friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Albus Dumbledore placed great trust in Hagrid, which Hagrid returned with fierce loyalty and unwavering admiration. This loyalty always flared up whenever someone insulted Dumbledore, one time causing Hagrid to give <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a> a pig's tail, and causing him to choke <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a> another time.
</p><p>While a professor, Dumbledore believed in Hagrid's innocence when he was accused of opening the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, and convinced then Headmaster, <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, to train Hagrid as the <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Gamekeeper</a> and allow him to remain at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-CoS_16-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CoS-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Hagrid went on to join Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> as an adult, and he was the one tasked with bringing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to Dumbledore after <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">James and Lily Potter</a> were murdered in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>. 
</p><p>Dumbledore also trusted him to move the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> from <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a> to the school and believed Hagrid could offer Harry as much protection as "a bunch" of Ministry <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> could while shopping in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_25-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Dumbledore gave Hagrid the difficult task of approaching the <a href="/wiki/Giant_colony" title="Giant colony">giant colonies</a> of the North and dissuading them joining forces with <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, knowing Hagrid was fully capable of the delicate handling required to court the <a href="/wiki/Gurg" title="Gurg">Gurg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Dumbledore additionally was the only one who supported Hagrid's decision to bring his giant half-brother <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a> with him back to Hogwarts after his mission to recruit the giants failed, allowing Grawp to stay in the Forbidden Forest and later having him sent to the mountains near Hogsmeade. After Albus Dumbledore's death, Hagrid was so devastated to the point that he was inconsolable, despite the best efforts of <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a> and even his half-brother Grawp.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">"<i>Well. Hello. Yeh must be Harry. Hello, Harry Potter. I’m Rubeus Hagrid. And I’m gonna be yer friend whether yeh like it or not. ’Cos yeh’ve had it tough, not that yeh know it yet. An’ yer gonna need friends. Now yeh best come with me, don’t yeh think?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid to baby Harry after the murder of the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potters</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, a good friend and student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry Potter and Hagrid shared a special relationship. Hagrid was one of the first people (if not the first) Harry could remember showing him genuine kindness and appearing to truly care for him. Hagrid was the one who introduced Harry back into the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>, and he empathised with Harry's situation, as they were both a bit different from wizarding norm and were orphans who had been more or less left to fend for themselves. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Sent owls off ter all yer parents’ old school friends, askin’ fer photos . . . knew yeh didn’ have any . . . d’yeh like it?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid giving Harry a special <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_photo_album" title="Harry Potter&#39;s photo album">photo album</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hagrid was Harry's first true friend, and the two helped each other get through many difficult situations and constantly looked out for one another. Though Harry often took issue with Hagrid's penchant for collecting dangerous <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_pets" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s pets">pets</a>, as well as the fact Hagrid decided to bring his <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giant</a> <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">half-brother</a> to Hogwarts,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> he never failed to support Hagrid in his efforts to protect and care for all of them.   
</p><p>When Harry learned about Hagrid's half-giant status, he never showed any concern about it, citing his relationship to the Dursleys as an example of how people should not be judged by who they were related to but who they were themselves. Hagrid's kindness and friendship allowed Harry to come to terms with how being an orphan never leaves you, as Harry witnessed Hagrid still mourning his father's death even over fifty years since he passed. This bond between two orphans and Hagrid's reassurance that Harry's parents would be proud of him helped Harry to live with pride in his family. Hagrid was also the one who first told Harry about who his parents were and gave him his first true look at his heritage and family.  
</p><p>Hagrid was shocked and horrified when Harry came to Voldemort to be sacrificed and yelled at him to run. Hagrid was devastated when he thought Harry was dead and openly sobbed in front of the Death Eaters and rebuked the <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a> for not helping Harry. Hagrid returned Harry to the forest and was very gentle with his body. Hagrid was delighted when he found Harry was alive and was among the first people to congratulate Harry after he defeated Voldemort for the final time. 
</p><p>Hagrid also met <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> through Harry, and he presumably remained in touch with all three of them well after their time at Hogwarts, as in <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, Harry reminded his son, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a>, that he had been invited to <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_cabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s cabin">Hagrid's hut</a> for tea upon his arrival at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_26-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> In many ways, Hagrid served as a pillar of strength for Harry, giving him his first look at just how kind people can be, and gave Harry his first taste of kindness, which caught on like wildfire and served to groom Harry into the selfless guardian and warrior he became. Suffice it to say, were it not for Hagrid, Harry could have ended up a profoundly different person.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hermione_Granger_and_Ron_Weasley">Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Look, Hagrid's our friend, why don't we just go and ask him about it?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>That would be a cheerful visit. "Hello Hagrid! Tell us, have you been setting anything mad and hairy loose in the castle lately?"</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron about the monster in the Chamber of Secrets<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191008170323" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="336" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-image-key="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191008170323" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191008170323" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191008170323" decoding="async" width="250" height="336" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-image-key="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191008170323" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> Granger, his friends and students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Like <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, both Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley had a close relationship with the half-giant. Though Ron was openly outraged by some of Hagrid's more dangerous <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_pets" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s pets">pets</a>, particularly <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, Hermione was more reserved with her comments and tended to be more proactive than either Ron or Harry when it came to helping Hagrid protect his creatures. She tried desperately to help him appeal <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>'s death sentence in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_23-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and in her <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">fifth year</a>, she made every effort to ensure sure Hagrid's <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> curriculum would give <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> no excuse to sack him.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_17-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> revealed that Hagrid was half-giant in the <i>Daily Prophet</i>, both Ron and Hermione stood by him and convinced him that despite all the prejudice he faced, there were still people who loved him and wanted him to stay at the school. Hagrid was on the point of resigning, but with their encouragement, remained at Hogwarts and continued teaching. Ron did show a certain level of concern upon learning of Hagrid's shock, given wizarding history regarding giants; Hermione, on the other hand, noted in an unsurprising tone that she suspected it long ago, seeing as his size fit the profile.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_24-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hagrid came to Hermione's defence during her <a href="/wiki/1993%E2%80%931994_school_year" title="1993–1994 school year">third year</a> when she was in conflict with the boys (as Ron believed her <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">cat</a> had eaten his rat <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a>, and Harry was angry that she had gotten his <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_Firebolt" title="Harry Potter&#39;s Firebolt">Firebolt</a> confiscated). Hagrid was able to convince Harry and Ron of how poorly they were treating their friend, and eventually, he succeeded in getting the two to reconcile with Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_23-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> He also encouraged Hermione during her <a href="/wiki/1994-1995_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1994-1995 school year">fourth year</a> to ignore the hate mail as he had following Rita Skeeter releasing a nasty article about Hermione in <i><a href="/wiki/Witch_Weekly" title="Witch Weekly">Witch Weekly</a></i>.
It is possible that Hagrid was close with Ron and Hermione's daughter, <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose Granger-Weasley</a> and their son <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo Granger-Weasley</a>, as he was planning to have tea with Harry's son, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a>, in <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Madame_Olympe_Maxime">Madame Olympe Maxime</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Madame Olympe Maxime">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Madame Olympe Maxime"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Hagrid</b>: "<i>So…anyway…enough abou' me. What about you? Which side you got it on?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Madame Maxime</b>: "<i>It is chilly. I think I will go in now</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hagrid</b>: "<i>Eh? No, don' go! I've — I've never met another one before</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Madame Maxime</b>: "<i>Anuzzer </i>what<i>, precisely?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hagrid</b>: "<i>Another half-giant, o' course</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Madame Maxime</b>: "'<i>Ow dare you!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hagrid and Madame Maxime<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/Oympe_Maxime.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100129193615" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="237" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Oympe Maxime.jpg" data-image-key="Oympe_Maxime.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/Oympe_Maxime.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100129193615" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/Oympe_Maxime.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100129193615" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/Oympe_Maxime.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100129193615" decoding="async" width="180" height="237" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Oympe Maxime.jpg" data-image-key="Oympe_Maxime.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/Oympe_Maxime.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100129193615" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Oympe_Maxime.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, Hagrid began a romantic relationship with Madame Olympe Maxime, Headmistress of <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy</a>. They were often seen together, talking and walking around the grounds, and they danced together at the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>. Though the two had a minor falling-out when Hagrid implied (correctly) that Maxime, like him, was part-<a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giant</a>, they eventually reconciled and travelled together to appeal to the giants of the Northern <a href="/wiki/Giant_colony" title="Giant colony">colonies</a> and dissuade them from joining forces with <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>. Maxime was also seen comforting Hagrid during <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">funeral</a>. The current status of their relationship is unknown, but as Hagrid never got married, it can be assumed that their relationship did not work out.<sup id="cite_ref-Carnegie_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Carnegie-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Tom_Riddle/Lord_Voldemort"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tom_Riddle.2FLord_Voldemort">Tom Riddle/Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Tom Riddle/Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Tom Riddle/Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Monsters don’t make good pets, Hagrid.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Riddle before he turned Hagrid in<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100706215126" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom Riddle (16 years old).jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_(16_years_old).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706215126" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100706215126" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706215126" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom Riddle (16 years old).jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_(16_years_old).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Tom_Riddle_%2816_years_old%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706215126" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_Riddle_(16_years_old).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was two years below <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, and in Hagrid's <a href="/wiki/1940s" title="1940s">third year</a>, Riddle opened the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, unleashing a <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Basilisk</a> on <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students. After the death of <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Myrtle Warren</a>, Hogwarts was in danger of closing, and to prevent that happening, Riddle framed Hagrid and his pet <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, for the crime. Hagrid protected Aragog from Riddle, throwing him to the ground when he tried to curse Aragog, making Hagrid the only person to challenge Riddle while he was a student. Despite this, Hagrid was expelled from Hogwarts and had his <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_wand" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s wand">wand</a> snapped in half by the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CoS_16-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CoS-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Believing in Hagrid's innocence, however, Professor <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> convinced Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a> to allow Hagrid to stay on at Hogwarts as <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Gamekeeper</a>.
</p><p>Tom Riddle never felt remorse for framing Hagrid and ruining his life. As Riddle went on to become Lord Voldemort, Hagrid joined the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> to fight against Voldemort and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, Hagrid was devastated by the <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">murder</a> of his friends <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">James and Lily Potter</a> but was relieved when the Dark Lord disappeared after failing to kill young <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Although many thought that Voldemort was dead, Hagrid, agreeing with Dumbledore, believed that he would return one day, as he believed that he did not "<i>have enough human left in him to die</i>". As with most of the wizarding community, he refused to speak Voldemort's name, and generally referred to him as "You-Know-Who." However, when he first explained Voldemort's background to Harry, he reluctantly said Voldemort's name. When Voldemort was searching for the Philosopher's Stone, he took advantage of Hagrid's love and knowledge of magical creatures and through Quirinus Quirrell, gathered the secret of subduing <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a> through music from a drunken Hagrid, who was remorseful afterwards. Since Voldemort had a certain respect for Hogwart's professors, it is not known if that included Hagrid, who taught <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>. This is unlikely considering Hagrid's half-giant status.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, after his resurrection, Voldemort dispatched his Death Eaters to convince the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giants</a> to join their side, while Dumbledore had sent Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a> to do the same. While Hagrid and Maxime were on good terms with the Gurg, <a href="/wiki/Karkus" title="Karkus">Karkus</a>, the Death Eaters supported the giant <a href="/wiki/Golgomath" title="Golgomath">Golgomath</a> in an uprising that resulted in Golgomath beheading Karkus and taking over the giant colony. The giants then attacked Hagrid and Maxime, who were forced to retreat.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Hagrid fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and was captured by the Death Eaters. After Harry sacrificed himself to be killed, Voldemort ordered a grieving Hagrid to carry his friend's "dead" body in his arms, where it would be clearly visible to Harry's supporters. On the way back to the school, Hagrid expressed his fury with the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">centaurs</a> for staying out of the fight, prompting them to join in soon after.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_26-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Hagrid was among the first to congratulate Harry after his defeat of Voldemort, showing his disdain for the Dark Lord. It was never confirmed if he knew or would know that his former classmate and the Dark Lord were one and the same, however, since Hagrid said to Harry in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> that Voldemort was in Slytherin, it is likely that Hagrid knew.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Weasley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Weasley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Another Weasley, eh?... I spent half me life chasin' yer twin brothers away from the Forest!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hagrid to Ron when they first met<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Weasley family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was good friends with <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a>, though it is uncertain as to when they first met, Arthur and Molly not having been in the original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. He was most likely assistant or co- gamekeeper when Mr and Mrs Weasley were at school, because of the Ogg timeline discrepancy.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Arthur and Molly would have attended nearly two decades later (1960s). He met them again in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, at <a href="/wiki/Flourish_and_Blotts" title="Flourish and Blotts">Flourish and Blotts</a>, when Arthur got into a fist fight with <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>. Hagrid broke up the fight and told Arthur that he should have ignored Malfoy, though he clearly sympathised with Arthur on acting the feelings Malfoy went out of his way to inspire. Hagrid was fond of the Weasley's due to their kind nature, immense courage, and their fair-minded views on Muggle-borns and half-humans like himself. 
</p><p>Twins <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</a> were friends of Hagrid since their time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Hagrid seemed to be one of their favourite members of the staff, as he had a sense of humour and was not anywhere near as strict as many of the professors, though he mentioned that he spent "half his life" chasing the twins away from the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>.
Hagrid also knew <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charles Weasley</a> quite well; Charlie had been one of the best <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> students in his time at Hogwarts, and Hagrid described him as being "great with animals." He went on to study <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragons</a> in <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>, and Hagrid helped him with the dragons imported to <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>. Two years earlier, Hagrid had sent his pet dragon, "<a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a>" to Charlie in <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>, and Charlie later informed Hagrid that "Norbert" was, in fact, actually "Norberta."
</p><p><a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> also attended Hogwarts before working in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> with <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a>, and Hagrid encountered him numerous times when he moved back to <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>. Bill arrived with the Order of the Phoenix at Hogwarts during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, where he was attacked by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. Hagrid was invited to Bill's wedding to <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, in which <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>, the youngest child and only daughter of the Weasley family, was a bridesmaid. Hagrid was quite fond of Ginny throughout her time at Hogwarts, and she was among the students who never even considered turning her back on Hagrid when she found out he was half-giant. Hagrid also knew she had a crush on <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, and playfully teased Harry about the fact in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>.
</p><p>Hagrid did not appear to have much of a relationship with <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a>, though it is unlikely they would have been very close before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, even if they had had more contact. Though neither Ron, Harry, nor Hermione were likely to inform Hagrid of this, Percy wrote to his younger brother, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, upon finding out that Ron had been made a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a>, and advised him against associating with Hagrid, as he was a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>. He also tried to persuade Ron to support the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, in favour of Dumbledore, to whom Hagrid was fiercely loyal. However, Percy abandoned the Ministry once it fell to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, apologised to his family, and fought against the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, after which Hagrid would have undoubtedly thought better of him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="James_and_Lily_Potter">James and Lily Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: James and Lily Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: James and Lily Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>A car crash killed Lily and James Potter??? It’s an outrage! A scandal!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagrid defending Lily and James<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090727171514" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lily and James Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090727171514" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090727171514" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090727171514" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lily and James Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090727171514" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">James and Lily Potter</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid had been a good friend of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s parents, Lily and James, since the time they attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Hagrid admired them for being amongst the best wizards and witches of their age. Hagrid became a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> around the same time as James and Lily, and they fought together throughout the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. Hagrid was beside himself when Lily and James were <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">killed</a> in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>; <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> sent him to rescue their infant child, Harry, from the wreckage of their home in <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>, and Hagrid later reintroduced Harry to the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>.   
</p><p>Hagrid knew them very well and conveyed the truth about them to their son, who had been lead to believe insulting lies about them and their deaths, restoring and preserving their legacy in their son. Hagrid also kept a leather-bound family album of them which he gave to Harry, which Hagrid came into possession of through unknown circumstances, but might have been entrusted to him by Lily and James to give to their son. Hagrid was known to respect them for their desire to fight for what was right.  
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sirius_Black">Sirius Black</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sirius Black">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Sirius Black"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Look ... I knew Sirius longer 'n yeh did ... he died in battle, an' tha's the way he'd've wanted ter go -</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Rubeus Hagrid to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> on <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150104115719" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo Sirius Black 01 brown.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150104115719" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150104115719" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150104115719" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo Sirius Black 01 brown.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150104115719" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_Sirius_Black_01_brown.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Though Hagrid described <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> as having been a "trouble-maker" in his youth, Hagrid had clearly been fond of him, as well as his best friend, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, when they were students at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. After graduating, Sirius, along with James, <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J.
