Potter">Lily Evans</a>, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, joined the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> around the same time as Hagrid. 
</p><p>When James and Lily discovered they were <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s next targets, they went into to hiding with the use of the <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a>; Peter Pettigrew had been made their <a href="/wiki/Secret-Keeper" class="mw-redirect" title="Secret-Keeper">Secret-Keeper</a>, unbeknownst to anyone else, and betrayed the Potters to Voldemort, framing Sirius for the crime. For many years, everybody, including Hagrid, believed Sirius was the betrayer. The night James and Lily died, Hagrid met Sirius in <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>, where Hagrid had been sent to rescue the infant <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> from the wreckage of the Potter's destroyed home, and Sirius lent Hagrid his <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black%27s_motorbike" class="mw-redirect" title="Sirius Black&#39;s motorbike">flying motorbike</a> to deliver Harry to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. By <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, Hagrid was horrified to think that he comforted the "murdering traitor" that very night and deeply resented him for his betrayal, raging that had he knew, he would have attacked Black in retaliation.
</p><p>Hagrid learned the truth in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> once Voldemort returned, a year after Sirius escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and exposed Pettigrew as having been in hiding as <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>'s pet rat, Scabbers. When Harry and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> helped Sirius avoid the fate of receiving the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a>, they also saved <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>, who was poised for execution as ordered by the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, and in doing so, provided Sirius with transportation to make his escape.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_23-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore re-instated the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, and following Sirius' tragic death during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Harry inherited Buckbeak, whom he sent back into Hagrid's care at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_25-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Hagrid was saddened by Sirius's death and tried to comfort Harry the best he could, saying that having known Sirius, he was confident that Sirius wanted to go down the way he did, which he truly deemed a valiant way to die.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Remus Lupin</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid would have known Remus Lupin for about as long as he knew <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">the Potters</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, though they did not appear to be particularly close until <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> when Lupin was appointed <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, and they became co-workers. Both Hagrid and Lupin knew what it was like to be within the wizarding community, yet still considered outsiders and face its prejudices, as Lupin was a werewolf and Hagrid was a half-giant.
In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, they both joined the re-instated <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and worked together throughout the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> to protect <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and bring about the end of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid greatly respected <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> professor and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Gryffindor_House" title="Head of Gryffindor House">Head of Gryffindor House</a>. They attended Hogwarts around the same time (Hagrid having been expelled a few years before she started) and they later became members of the Hogwarts staff. As one of the most strict professors at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, McGonagall sometimes disapproved of Hagrid's lack of refined behaviour, especially during the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a>. However, they were close friends and fellow members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> in both wars.  
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, when <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> brought several <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> officials to either have Hagrid forcibly removed from the school grounds, arrested, or both, McGonagall immediately came to Hagrid's defence; she took four simultaneous <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunners</a> straight to her chest as she rushed to Hagrid's aid, and was incapacitated for some time at <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>. Hagrid was disgusted when McGonagall got stunned to the point that he attacked the Ministry officials who injured her in an uncontrollable rage, furiously denouncing them as cowards.  
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s death, McGonagall stated that she appreciated Hagrid's opinion very much, as Dumbledore had, and took it into consideration when determining the best time to close the school. McGonagall later became Headmistress of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, where Hagrid was still living by <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>. Also, McGonagall showed no disdain when Hagrid drunkenly kissed her on the cheek at a Hogwarts Christmas celebration. On the contrary, she began to giggle and blushed. McGonagall was touched by Hagrid's defence of wanting to bury their mentor, Albus Dumbledore on Hogwarts's grounds, citing that no other Headmaster had given more to the school, and as such defended his stance on the matter. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150307193047" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="269" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150307193047" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150307193047" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150307193047" decoding="async" width="180" height="269" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150307193047" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid always stoutly defended <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> against Harry's doubts and allegations, on the basis that <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> trusted Snape completely. When Snape killed Dumbledore, Hagrid initially disbelieved the fact and told Harry he must be mistaken but was later furious to learn that Snape had indeed killed the late Headmaster. Hagrid openly opposed Snape when he became the Headmaster of Hogwarts by holding a <a href="/wiki/Support_Harry_Potter_party" title="Support Harry Potter party">Support Harry Potter party</a> (unaware Snape was secretly still on their side), an act which almost resulted in his arrest and forced him to go into hiding until the final battle. Before Hagrid fled, Snape put students in detentions with Hagrid, ensuring that they were protected from the harsher and torturous punishments from the <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Carrows</a>. However, Hagrid eventually learned of Snape's true loyalties during the final confrontation of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> regularly found themselves at odds; Filch thought that Hagrid was "an oaf," and even told <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a>, his cat, to keep an eye on the Gateskeeper. Filch did not seem to care or even really acknowledge when Hagrid became a professor, possibly because he was a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>, and Hagrid, for his part, called Filch a "sneakin' Squib", when the latter insulted him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20061208054304" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="200" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg" data-image-key="Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20061208054304" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20061208054304" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20061208054304" decoding="async" width="180" height="200" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg" data-image-key="Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20061208054304" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Firenzeinharrypotter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The centaur <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid had been very familiar with Divination Professor <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a>, long before he began working at Hogwarts, and when the centaur's <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">herd</a> turned on him for entering into "the servitude of a human" by accepting the position at Hogwarts as a favour to Headmaster Dumbledore, it was Hagrid who saved him. Of all the centaurs Firenze seemed to be the most active in working against Lord Voldemort and was not above allowing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to ride on his back in the process of saving Harry's life — both of which elicited great respect and gratitude from both Harry and Hagrid.
</p><p>Hagrid also seemed to be on good terms with <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">master</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>. It is possible that Slughorn was one of Hagrid's teachers at Hogwarts, but they later became co-workers. Slughorn attended <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>'s funeral and comforted Hagrid, and while this was mostly because he wanted to extract some of Aragog's valuable venom, Hagrid was touched nonetheless, and the two enjoyed a drunken salute to the late <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>.
</p><p>Hagrid initially held <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> in high regard, considering him a very talented and clever wizard, and initially seemed to have a good relationship with him, especially when he introduced Quirrell to Harry in the Leaky Cauldron. However, due to his loyalty to Voldemort, a disguised Quirrell later took advantage of Hagrid's love for magical creatures and manipulated a drunken Hagrid into revealing the secret of getting past Fluffy in exchange for a <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">dragon egg</a>. Hagrid was later horrified and guilt-ridden when he learnt of Quirrell's true nature after his death, calling him an "evil git" and blaming himself for Harry's injuries during his encounter with Quirrell and Voldemort. 
</p><p>Hagrid had a mixed relationship with <a href="/wiki/Wilhelmina_Grubbly-Plank" title="Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank">Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank</a> as while she worked as a substitute for Hagrid in Care for Magical Creatures and his gamekeeping duties when Hagrid was absent or had a mission to do, he slightly envied her teaching skills, which made other students (including Harry, Ron and Hermione) consider her a superior teacher to him for Care of Magical Creatures. This also made him accept Harry, Ron and Hermione's untrue claims of Grubby-Plank being a "terrible teacher" when they attempted to reassure him that they still cared for him despite not taking the subject for their sixth year. Grubbly-Plank on the other hand seemed to respect Hagrid for his skills and abilities despite the students considering her a better teacher than him, as she complimented Hagrid's training of the school's Thestrals and also kept silent about his mission to recruit the giants when Harry inquired her about his whereabouts, understanding the importance of his classified mission. 
</p><p>Hagrid disliked <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, as did the other teachers, due to his being an obnoxious and annoyingly incompetent teacher. Hagrid did not read any of Lockhart's books, rejected his ideas of Harry trying to hog the spotlight, and openly criticised him, something that he would not normally do to a teacher.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="238" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" decoding="async" width="180" height="238" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The professor with whom Hagrid had the most difficult and antagonistic relationship was, by far, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, who was a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">pure-blood supremacist</a> with a particular dislike for what she called "<a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a>." Throughout the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">1995–1996 school year</a>, she made Hagrid's life miserable with her disruptive evaluations of his teaching (part of her role as <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">Hogwarts High Inquisitor</a>, during which she was unabashedly condescending and critical.) 
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jordan" title="Lee Jordan">a student</a> released two <a href="/wiki/Niffler" title="Niffler">nifflers</a> in her office, following Headmaster Dumbledore's departure from the school, she blamed Hagrid, although he had a rock solid alibi. She later brought <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> officials to <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_cabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s cabin">Hagrid's hut</a> in the middle of the night, either to arrest or forcibly remove him from the premises, though Hagrid was able to resist with the help of <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> and go on the run. 
</p><p>Hagrid was disgusted by Umbridge's and the officials attack on McGonagall, attacking the Ministry officials in retaliation, although he refrained from attacking Umbridge in order to escape from Hogwarts. Following the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_in_the_Forbidden_Forest" title="Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest">Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest</a>, Umbridge was eventually suspended from Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a> and Hagrid was reinstated as a teacher. She was also imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> two years later for her crimes against <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-Born">Muggle-Borns</a> because of her actions as <a href="/wiki/Head_of_the_Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Head of the Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Head of the Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_students">Hogwarts students</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts students">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Hogwarts students"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Apart from Harry, Ron and Hermione and the other Weasley children (excluding Percy), Hagrid seemed to have a good relationship with <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jordan" title="Lee Jordan">Lee Jordan</a> who was a friend of <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</a> as he once shook Hagrid's hand, along with Fred and George, when he returned after his mission to find the giants. Apart from them, the other students had a mixed relationship with Hagrid which was especially evident while he taught <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>. 
</p><p>Although many of the students had a relatively civil relationship with Hagrid outside his teaching, most of them considered Professor <a href="/wiki/Grubbly-Plank" class="mw-redirect" title="Grubbly-Plank">Grubbly-Plank</a> a more qualified teacher for the subject since Hagrid sometimes lost his confidence and preferred teaching dangerous creatures. The <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students expressed the most enthusiasm when he assumed the post but after Draco Malfoy caused Buckbeak to attack him by insulting him and when Hagrid preferred teaching monstrous creatures over creatures which were tame, their enthusiasm on the subject reduced. Despite this, Hagrid arguably had the best relationship with the Gryffindor students as he was once a Gryffindor himself and was regularly seen supporting Gryffindor during Quiddich matches alongside the other Gryffindor students. <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> believed that Hagrid was a poor teacher and said that <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> students considered him a joke. It is unknown what relationship Hagrid had with the <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> students, although it is possible their relationship was also mixed like the other students. However, while the other students mostly disapproved his teaching methods, Hagrid had an antagonistic relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students as they, encouraged by Draco Malfoy, were also prejudiced against Hagrid due to his status as a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>, and Draco's attack by Buckbeak, without caring that Draco did not listen to Hagrid in the first place.
</p><p>However, despite Hagrid's mixed relationship with them, most of the students with the exception of Slytherin opposed Dolores Umbridge alongside Hagrid and disapproved of Umbridge's harsh and critical treatment of Hagrid due to her prejudice against part-humans. They also believed that Hagrid had improved in his teaching by the time he was temporarily sacked by Umbridge although many of them did not take the subject for <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.Ts</a> due to their past experiences with the dangerous creatures he taught. They were also extremely angry when Hagrid was attacked by Umbridge, again excluding the Slytherin students. Hagrid also opposed the Death Eater's control of Hogwarts alongside many of the students, including holding a Support Harry Potter Party in his Hut, and also fought alongside them against Voldemort and the Death Eater's during the Battle of Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dursley_family">Dursley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dursley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Dursley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Vernon Dursley</b>: "<i>I demand that you leave at once, sir! You are breaking and entering!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Rubeus Hagrid</b>: "<i>Ah, shut up, Dursley, yeh great prune.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hagird insulting Vernon Dursley<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/Dursley_family_%28Promotional_photo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161220012743" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="266" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dursley family (Promotional photo).jpg" data-image-key="Dursley_family_(Promotional_photo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/Dursley_family_%28Promotional_photo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161220012743" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/Dursley_family_%28Promotional_photo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161220012743" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/Dursley_family_%28Promotional_photo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161220012743" decoding="async" width="250" height="266" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dursley family (Promotional photo).jpg" data-image-key="Dursley_family_(Promotional_photo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/Dursley_family_%28Promotional_photo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161220012743" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dursley_family_(Promotional_photo).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Vernon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Hagrid was sent by Albus Dumbledore to inform Harry Potter of his true identity on Harry's <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_eleventh_birthday" title="Harry Potter&#39;s eleventh birthday">eleventh birthday</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> after it was revealed that Hogwarts' letters to him were getting blocked by his aunt and uncle, Vernon and Petunia Dursley, both <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a> who hated and feared magic. 
</p><p>Eventually, Hagrid found Harry and his family in <a href="/wiki/Hut-on-the-Rock" title="Hut-on-the-Rock">an old shack</a> out at sea (Vernon Dursley had become paranoid with the amount of Hogwarts letters arriving at their home, so he had temporarily vacated their home in the hopes that they would throw off any wizards possibly following them.) After giving Harry a birthday cake, he introduced himself to Harry, believing him to know everything about the wizarding world (from <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_letter_to_Petunia_Dursley" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s letter to Petunia Dursley">the letter left by Albus Dumbledore</a>.) Upon learning that Harry knew nothing, Hagrid became furious at the Dursleys for not telling him anything. 
</p><p>When Hagrid proceeded to tell Harry that he was a wizard, Vernon became angry and admitted that they had known for years and had been trying to "stomp it out of him", including admitting that they lied to Harry in telling him that his parents had really been killed in a car crash. This further enraged Hagrid, but Vernon continued to try and keep Harry from going to Hogwarts, going so far as to call Albus Dumbledore a "crackpot old fool". This, however, sent Hagrid over the edge; he lost his temper and used his pink <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_umbrella" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s umbrella">umbrella</a> to give Dudley Dursley a pig's tail. This terrified Vernon and Petunia enough to let Hagrid take Harry. Eventually, they would remove the pig tail, but the encounter added a newfound fear of magic to the Dursleys' hatred of it. The incident scared Dudley so much that he instinctively grabbed his bottom when meeting the Weasleys, despite them being friendly wizards.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Malfoy_family">Malfoy family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Malfoy family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Malfoy family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Yeh should’ve ignored him, Arthur. Rotten ter the core, the whole family, everyone knows that — no Malfoy’s worth listenin’ ter — bad blood, that’s what it is — </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hagird's scathing opinion of the Malfoy family<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080512050348" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="349" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoys.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080512050348" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080512050348" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080512050348" decoding="async" width="250" height="349" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoys.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080512050348" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoys.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucius and Draco Malfoy, his enemies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was disgusted by the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy family</a>'s pure blood supremacist values, their open ill-treatment of <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> and "<a href="/wiki/Blood_traitor" title="Blood traitor">blood traitors</a>," their allegiance to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and their disrespect to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. In turn, the Malfoys disliked Hagrid, regularly mocking him and doing nearly everything in their collective power to get him sacked from his post at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, Hagrid broke up a fight between <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Flourish_and_Blotts" title="Flourish and Blotts">Flourish and Blotts</a>, though Hagrid was quite understanding of what Arthur had felt the need to do. During the <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_school_year" title="1992–1993 school year">1992–1993 school year</a>, Lucius was indirectly responsible for reopening of the Chamber of Secrets, as he had used the earlier scuffle with Arthur Weasley to slip <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s diary">Tom Riddle's diary</a> into <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>'s cauldron full of books. Hagrid was blamed for the attacks, just as he had been fifty years earlier when he was framed by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> for the Chamber's first opening. Hagrid was arrested as a precautionary measure by <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, where Hagrid reacted angrily to Lucius' unnecessary presence and ordered him to get out his house. Lucius mocked Hagrid by wondering how his small hut could be considered a "house" and claimed he was only there to inform <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> that he and the other governors had voted on his suspension. Hagrid saw through Lucius and accused him of threatening the other governors, which later proved to have been exactly the case.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>What're you doin' here? Get outta my house!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Rubeus Hagrid to <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hagrid did not get along any better with Lucius’ son <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a>. Even before meeting Hagrid for the first time, Draco slandered him when talking to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> for the first time, describing him as "...a sort of savage - lives in a hut in the school grounds and every now and then he gets drunk, tries to do magic and ends up setting fire to his bed." Hagrid first met Draco in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> when he was sorted into Slytherin. During that year, Draco was put in detention with Harry Potter, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>. Hagrid called Draco an "idiot" when he scared Neville, and in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, was outraged when he heard Draco called Hermione a Mudblood. Draco was in Hagrid’s <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> class in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> and ignored Hagrid’s advice on how to handle Hagrid’s <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriff</a> <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>. Draco insulted Buckbeak, causing the hippogriff to lash out and cut Draco’s arm. Hagrid took Draco to the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a>, but Draco swore revenge, and deliberately exaggerated his injury to get Hagrid into trouble. Lucius was furious when he found out and took legal action against Hagrid and Buckbeak. Hagrid tried hard to defend Buckbeak, but the court ruled in favour of Lucius, largely due to his influence at the Ministry, and Buckbeak was sentenced to death, though thanks to the efforts of Harry and Hermione, Buckbeak managed to escape. 
</p><p>In Draco's fourth year, he openly disobeyed Hagrid by saying that he would not be coming down to look after the blast-ended skrewts, saying that he spent too much time with them during regular class. Hagrid, hearing about the previous punishment 'Moody' gave Draco, threatened to turn him into a ferret. Later that year, Draco happily provided <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> with skewed details about the events of the previous year and delighted when Hagrid temporarily went into hiding following Skeeter's publication of the article revealing that Hagrid was half-giant. In his fifth year, Draco spoke negatively regarding Hagrid during <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>'s inspection of a Care of Magical Creatures class conducted by <a href="/wiki/Wilhelmina_Grubbly-Plank" title="Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank">Professor Grubbly-Plank</a>, likely hoping that Hagrid would be placed on <a href="/wiki/Probation" title="Probation">probation</a> when and if he returned to Hogwarts, an outcome that did indeed come to pass.
</p><p>Given that Draco's wife Astoria helped to raise their son to be a kinder man than Draco was in his youth, it can be assumed that Scorpius Malfoy had a better relationship with Hagrid than his father did. This is also likely due to Scorpius being best friends with Albus Potter who was already a good friend of Hagrid's before his first year. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix_members">Order of the Phoenix members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=40" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix members"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hagrid was friendly with most members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Some of them were <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">James and Lily Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>.
</p><p>Hagrid also knew and greatly admired <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, and Moody's protege, <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>. They fought together in several battles, including the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, where Hagrid was devastated by Moody's death. Tonks later married <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, and their son, Teddy, would attend <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> after both his parents were killed at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>Hagrid was also familiar with <a href="/wiki/Dedalus_Diggle" title="Dedalus Diggle">Dedalus Diggle</a>, whom he introduced to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Death_Eaters_and_enemies">Death Eaters and enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=41" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Death Eaters and enemies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Death Eaters and enemies"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110418214318" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH2 Death Eaters with Voldemort during the battle.jpg" data-image-key="DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110418214318" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110418214318" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110418214318" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH2 Death Eaters with Voldemort during the battle.jpg" data-image-key="DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110418214318" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH2_Death_Eaters_with_Voldemort_during_the_battle.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort and his Death Eaters in the Forbidden Forest</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Hagrid was a member of the Order of the Phoenix, he disliked the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and tried to thwart their plans most of the time. The Death Eaters whom Hagrid knew the most were <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> and his son <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a>, clashing with Lucius before he was put in Azkaban, and had clashes with Draco while he taught Care of Magical Creatures.
</p><p>Snape, on the other hand, defected from Voldemort and Hagrid defended him whenever Harry, Ron and Hermione criticised him, except when he temporarily believed that Snape betrayed Dumbledore by killing him before learning of his true loyalties in the final battle.
</p><p>Apart from the Malfoys, Hagrid also had an antagonistic relationship with <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a> as they clashed when Buckbeak was going to be executed, when Macnair persuaded the giants to join Voldemort, and during the Battle of Hogwarts when Hagrid threw him across the Great Hall, knocking him unconscious. Hagrid also knew <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a>, as he once choked Karkaroff against a tree and told him to apologise to Dumbledore when he spat on him and accused him of an <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">attack</a> on <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>. <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a> also tried to attack Hagrid following the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle at Astronomy Tower</a> and set his hut on fire. He later angrily silenced Hagrid when the latter tried to discourage <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> from sacrificing himself.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Rubeus, possibly from the Latin word "rubinus", means "red." According to Rowling herself, the first names of Albus Dumbledore and Rubeus Hagrid were chosen based on "the white" and "the red", which were considered essential mystical components of <a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">alchemy</a>. Hagrid was given the red for passion or emotion, "an earthy, warm and physical man, lord of the forest".<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorecolours_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorecolours-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Hagride is a verb that means "to torment".</li>
<li>Hagrid also may mean "hung over," as from <a href="/wiki/Alcohol" title="Alcohol">alcohol</a>.</li>
<li>A hag is a nightmare spirit in English folklore. According to folklore, the Hag sat on a sleeper's chest and sent nightmares to him or her. When the subject awoke, he or she would be unable to breathe or even move for a short period of time. This state is now called sleep paralysis, but in the old belief the subject had been "hagridden".<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>His name (and Dumbledore's) come from a passage in chapter 20 of the <i>Mayor of Casterbridge </i>by Thomas Hardy. "Hag-rids" (as it is in the <i>Mayor of Casterbridge</i>) referred to indigestion.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/HagridSad.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080323222557" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="233" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HagridSad.jpg" data-image-key="HagridSad.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/HagridSad.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080323222557" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/HagridSad.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080323222557" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/HagridSad.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080323222557" decoding="async" width="180" height="233" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HagridSad.jpg" data-image-key="HagridSad.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/HagridSad.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080323222557" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HagridSad.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid as illustrated by <a href="/wiki/Mary_GrandPr%C3%A9" title="Mary GrandPré">Mary GrandPré</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/HagridWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200715130117" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="378" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HagridWU.png" data-image-key="HagridWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/HagridWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200715130117" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/HagridWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200715130117" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/HagridWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200715130117" decoding="async" width="180" height="378" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HagridWU.png" data-image-key="HagridWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/HagridWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200715130117" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HagridWU.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid as he appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Wizards_Unite" title="Harry Potter: Wizards Unite">Harry Potter: Wizards Unite</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Hagrid was the first person to tell Harry that he resembled his father, but had his mother's eyes. He was also Harry's first friend.</li>
<li>It is unknown why no one calls Hagrid 'Rubeus', which is his first name, although when Hagrid meets Harry for the first time he tells him to call him Hagrid as that's what everyone calls him. This probably means that Hagrid tells people to call him by this name. The only individuals known to call Hagrid by his first name were Garrick Ollivander and Tom Riddle, who have both known him since he was a child.</li>
<li>Given Hagrid's interest in unusual pets, it is possible that his activities may have caught the eye of the <a href="/wiki/Illegal_Pets_Detection" title="Illegal Pets Detection">Illegal Pets Detection</a> service at some point.</li>
<li>Hagrid was not charged for raising Aragog under the <a href="/wiki/Ban_on_Experimental_Breeding" title="Ban on Experimental Breeding">Ban on Experimental Breeding</a> because it was enacted in <a href="/wiki/1965" title="1965">1965</a>, 22 years later.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110626104957" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Robbie Coltrane as Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110626104957" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110626104957" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110626104957" decoding="async" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Robbie Coltrane as Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110626104957" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Robbie_Coltrane_as_Hagrid.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Robbie Coltrane as Hagrid</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Hagrid is portrayed by Scottish actor <a href="/wiki/Robbie_Coltrane" title="Robbie Coltrane">Robbie Coltrane</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Part 2</a></i> and so is one of the 14 characters to appear in all 8 film adaptations.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Robbie_Coltrane" title="Robbie Coltrane">Robbie Coltrane</a> was J. K. Rowling's first and only choice for the role of Rubeus Hagrid. She did not, however, create the character with Robbie Coltrane in mind. He was instead, according to Coltrane, "based on a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hell%27s_Angels" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Hell&#39;s Angels">Hell's Angel</a> she knew in the <a href="/wiki/West_Country" title="West Country">West Country</a>. ...he was just huge and terrifying. And then he would sit down and talk about his garden and how his petunias had been very bad that year."<sup id="cite_ref-pts29_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pts29-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> This is the reason why Coltrane is the only known actor to not speak in their native accent, instead speaking in a West Country accent, which is the only English accent noted for rolling of the 'r' sound, and often silencing 'h' sounds, which also became a stereotypical accent of pirates, because Robert Newton, who played the main character on Treasure Island, is actually from Devon in southwestern England.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>As well as being Rowling's first choice for the role of Hagrid, Coltrane was also the first person cast in the movie. Interestingly, Coltrane is one of the few actors to play a character <i>older</i> than themselves (Hagrid is in his 60s throughout the series, whilst Coltrane was 51 when he first played Hagrid and 61 the last time he did.)</li>
<li>American actor Robin Williams wanted the role of Hagrid and called director <a href="/wiki/Chris_Columbus" title="Chris Columbus">Chris Columbus</a> as well as casting director <a class="new" title="Janet Hirshenson (page does not exist)" rel="nofollow" data-uncrawlable-url="L3dpa2kvSmFuZXRfSGlyc2hlbnNvbj9hY3Rpb249ZWRpdCZyZWRsaW5rPTE=">Janet Hirshenson</a> if he could get the part.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wikipedia:Citing sources"><i><span title="The material in the vicinity of this tag needs references to reliable sources." style="white-space: nowrap;">citation needed</span></i></a>&#93;</sup> However, the <i>"strictly British and Irish cast"</i> rule imposed by J.K. Rowling prevented him from getting the role, and Columbus with Hirshenson had to reject him out of respect for Rowling's wishes.</li>
<li>Robbie Coltrane returned to the part of Hagrid in 2014 and shot 3 different scenes for the official <i>Wizarding World of Harry Potter </i>website on which Hagrid welcomes the viewer in the Diagon Alley expansion.</li></ul></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110130030231" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mfpmp 2011-01-29 22-00-32-19.jpg" data-image-key="Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110130030231" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110130030231" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110130030231" decoding="async" width="180" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mfpmp 2011-01-29 22-00-32-19.jpg" data-image-key="Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110130030231" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mfpmp_2011-01-29_22-00-32-19.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Robbie_Coltrane" title="Robbie Coltrane">Robbie Coltrane</a> was usually filmed from a low camera angle to make him appear larger</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Since Robbie Coltrane is not really 8-feet 6-inches tall, he was usually filmed from a low camera angle to make him look bigger (usually <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>'s angle) or the other actors are filmed from a high camera angle.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>Hagrid appears smaller in the films than in the novels, as the filmmakers describe him to be 8 feet 6 inches tall (as opposed to being 11 feet six inches in the books).</li>
<li>Curiously, it says on Hagrid's Ministry card that he is 11.5 feet tall and weighs 289 pounds. However, this would mean that he is dangerously underweight, as his Body Mass Index (BMI) is only 10.6. The only other known character to be below the range is <a href="/wiki/Porpentina_Goldstein" title="Porpentina Goldstein">Porpentina Goldstein</a> with a BMI of 17.8. The fact that Hagrid should be facing life-threatening symptoms from being all skin and bones is self-defeating: he is frequently described as huge and bulky in the books, and he is portrayed in the films by an obese actor (he weighed 280 pounds and was six feet tall).<sup id="cite_ref-LE_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LE-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> For Hagrid's weight to match his superhuman stature, he would like have to weigh in at over 1,000 pounds, as when you double an object's volume, you actually quadruple its weight to maintain structural integrity relative to the Earth's gravitational pull on its mass.</li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Martin_Bayfield" title="Martin Bayfield">Martin Bayfield</a> played Hagrid as a teenager during the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, and was dubbed by Robbie Coltrane. Bayfield also often served as the role of Hagrid's body double, wearing a prosthetic Hagrid suit, in scenes such as the final scene of the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i> in which Hagrid waved goodbye to Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-pts35_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pts35-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When Harry mentions Hagrid at the conclusion of Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows (novel), the year is 2017, and Hagrid is one year off turning 90 years old.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/HagridBirthdayCake.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080509015738" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HagridBirthdayCake.jpg" data-image-key="HagridBirthdayCake.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/HagridBirthdayCake.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080509015738" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/HagridBirthdayCake.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080509015738" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/HagridBirthdayCake.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080509015738" decoding="async" width="180" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HagridBirthdayCake.jpg" data-image-key="HagridBirthdayCake.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/HagridBirthdayCake.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080509015738" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HagridBirthdayCake.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hagrid's bad spelling: "<i>Happee Birthdae Harry</i>"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>:
<ul><li>Hagrid seems to have poor spelling, as seen when he shows Harry his birthday cake. In addition to this, when Hagrid tells Harry about how his parents were killed, Harry asked You-Know-Who's name. Hagrid responded he didn't want to say his name and when Harry suggested to write it down, Hagrid said he couldn't spell "Voldemort".</li>
<li>When Harry, Ron, and Hermione approached Hagrid to ask him about the Philosopher's Stone, Hagrid is playing the <i>Harry Potter</i> theme tune on his flute.</li></ul></li></ul>
<p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><figure class="thumb tright " style="width: 74px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Screenshot_754.png/revision/latest?cb=20150509205557" class="image"><img alt="Screenshot 754.png" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="72" height="70" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Screenshot 754.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_754.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Screenshot_754.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/72?cb=20150509205557" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Screenshot_754.png/revision/latest?cb=20150509205557" class="image"><img alt="Screenshot 754.png" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Screenshot_754.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/72?cb=20150509205557" decoding="async" width="72" height="70" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Screenshot 754.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_754.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Screenshot_754.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/72?cb=20150509205557" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 		 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p class="mw-empty-elt"></p>
<ul><li>Throughout the series, it is implied that Hagrid had been the Hogwarts <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">gatekeeper</a> since he was expelled from school in 1943. But at one point in <i>Goblet of Fire</i>, <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>, who attended Hogwarts between 1961 and 1968, reminisces about Hagrid's predecessor, <a href="/wiki/Ogg" title="Ogg">Ogg</a>, in contradiction to this implication. However, it is stated by Tom Riddle in <i>Chamber of Secrets</i> that Dumbledore persuaded Headmaster Dippet to keep Hagrid on as part of the staff and have him trained for the position, meaning he started out as Ogg's assistant.<figure class="thumb tright " style="width: 95px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Screenshot_1192.png/revision/latest?cb=20150502150215" class="image"><img alt="Screenshot 1192.png" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="93" height="81" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Screenshot 1192.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_1192.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Screenshot_1192.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/93?cb=20150502150215" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Screenshot_1192.png/revision/latest?cb=20150502150215" class="image"><img alt="Screenshot 1192.png" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Screenshot_1192.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/93?cb=20150502150215" decoding="async" width="93" height="81" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Screenshot 1192.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_1192.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Screenshot_1192.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/93?cb=20150502150215" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 		 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> states on her website that Hagrid is allergic to cats, as well as being hinted at in the first book, which could explain why he dislikes <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a> so much.</li>
<li>Hagrid's <a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter" title="LEGO Harry Potter">LEGO</a> mini-figure incarnations consist almost entirely of pieces exclusive only to Hagrid, specifically the body and beard pieces. His head in and of itself is not an exclusive piece, but his face pattern is.</li>
<li>Hagrid is a playable character in <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i>. In the game, he can <a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">fly</a> on a <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomstick</a> in the game in spite of the fact that he claims in the books to be too large to ride broomsticks.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Fans of the series raised an immediate outcry upon learning that Hagrid never married. J.K. Rowling responded to the criticism by simply saying, "At least I didn't kill him."</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i>, Hagrid is the first playable character, at the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a> in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>. As Hagrid was expelled, he only has one spell on his Spell-Wheel, which is Wingardium Leviosa. However, after the player makes it to Hogwarts, he obtains his crossbow. Hagrid is unlocked in "The Forbidden Forest" level, by using Reducto on a silver chest in the third area.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (video game)">video game adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, it was rumoured that Hagrid had an evil twin brother named <a href="/wiki/Dirgah_Hagrid" title="Dirgah Hagrid">Dirgah</a>.</li>
<li>In the credits of the film adaptation of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i> and in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1 (video game)">video game adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i>, Hagrid is listed as "Hagrid the Giant".</li>
<li>In the extended version of 'JK Rowling and Daniel Radcliffe - A conversation', it is revealed that Rubeus is pronounced Roo-Bay-Us. It is unknown why JK Rowling did not ask for this to be the same in the films, somewhat like Voldemort, which in the books is pronounced with a silent T, except in the British Audible Renditions and American Audible Renditions of the last 3 books.</li>
<li>In the novel <i>Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</i>, Hagrid was quoting "fool Gorgon" when he was about to sent a letter to Dumbledore regarding Harry at the first time he met him. Either Hagrid quoted that line as a mere cursing, or he knew that Gorgons (women-like creatures from Greek Mythology with living snakes as hair) existed in the magical world.</li></ul>
